# Run and deploy your AI Studio app

This contains everything you need to run your app locally.

View your app in AI Studio: https://ai.studio/apps/6fce1cee-a729-432c-a808-94c53064bb6b

## Run Locally

**Prerequisites:**  Node.js


1. Install dependencies:
   `npm install`
2. Set the `GEMINI_API_KEY` in [.env.local](.env.local) to your Gemini API key
3. Run the app:
   `npm run dev`

FILE: bridge.jsx
------------------------------------------------------------

(function () {
  try {
    if ($.global._aeHubSocket) $.global._aeHubSocket.close();
  } catch (e) {}

  $.global._aeHubSafeWrite = function (str) {
    var clean = str.replace(/[\r\n]/g, "");
    var max = 4000;
    for (var i = 0; i < clean.length; i += max) {
      $.global._aeHubSocket.write(clean.substring(i, i + max));
    }
    $.global._aeHubSocket.write("\n");
  };

  $.global._aeHubSocket = new Socket();
  $.global._aeHubBuffer = "";
  $.global._aeHubConnected = false;

  try {
    $.global._aeHubConnected = $.global._aeHubSocket.open(
      "127.0.0.1:8092",
      "utf-8",
    );
  } catch (e) {
    $.global._aeHubConnected = false;
  }

  if ($.global._aeHubConnected) {
    $.global._aeHubSocket.timeout = 0;
    $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(
      JSON.stringify({ type: "status", message: "bridge_connected" }),
    );

    $.global._aeHubPoll = function () {
      if (!$.global._aeHubConnected) return;
      try {
        var data = $.global._aeHubSocket.read();
        if (data && data.length > 0) {
          $.global._aeHubBuffer += data;
          var lines = $.global._aeHubBuffer.split("\n");
          $.global._aeHubBuffer = lines.pop();
          for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
            var line = lines[i].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
            if (!line) continue;
            try {
              var cmd = JSON.parse(line);
              var result = $.global._aeHubExec(cmd);
              $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(
                JSON.stringify({
                  type: "result",
                  reqId: cmd.reqId,
                  data: result,
                }),
              );
            } catch (e) {
              try {
                if (typeof cmd !== "undefined")
                  $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(
                    JSON.stringify({
                      type: "error",
                      reqId: cmd.reqId,
                      error: e.toString(),
                    }),
                  );
              } catch (e2) {}
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        $.global._aeHubConnected = false;
        return;
      }
      app.scheduleTask("_aeHubPoll()", 50, false);
    };

    $.global._aeHubSync = function () {
      if (!$.global._aeHubConnected) return;
      try {
        var activeComp = null;
        var comp = app.project ? app.project.activeItem : null;
        var comps = [];
        var layers = [];

        if (app.project) {
          for (var i = 1; i <= app.project.numItems; i++) {
            var item = app.project.item(i);
            if (item instanceof CompItem)
              comps.push({ id: item.id, name: item.name });
          }
        }

        if (comp && comp instanceof CompItem) {
          activeComp = {
            index: comp.itemIndex,
            id: comp.id,
            name: comp.name,
            width: comp.width,
            height: comp.height,
            duration: comp.duration,
            frameRate: comp.frameRate,
            numLayers: comp.numLayers,
            time: comp.time,
          };
          for (var j = 1; j <= Math.min(comp.numLayers, 50); j++) {
            var l = comp.layer(j);
            layers.push({
              index: j,
              name: l.name,
              selected: l.selected,
              enabled: l.enabled,
              locked: l.locked,
              hasVideo: l.hasVideo,
              hasAudio: l.hasAudio,
              audioEnabled: l.audioEnabled,
              solo: l.solo,
              type: $.global._aeHubGLT(l),
            });
          }
        }

        $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(
          JSON.stringify({
            type: "status",
            message: "sync",
            state: {
              activeComp: activeComp,
              layers: layers,
              compositions: comps,
            },
          }),
        );
      } catch (e) {}
      app.scheduleTask("_aeHubSync()", 1000, false);
    };

    $.global._aeHubExec = function (cmd) {
      switch (cmd.action) {
        case "ping":
          return { pong: true, time: new Date().toString() };
        case "getAppInfo":
          return {
            appName: app.appName,
            version: app.version,
            buildNumber: app.buildNumber,
            language: app.language,
            projectFile:
              app.project && app.project.file ? app.project.file.fsName : null,
            projectName: app.project ? app.project.name : null,
          };
        case "playPause":
          try {
            app.executeCommand(1045);
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.executeCommand(app.findMenuCommandId("Preview"));
            } catch (e2) {}
          }
          return { success: true };

        case "getComps":
          var comps = [];
          if (!app.project) return { comps: comps };
          for (var i = 1; i <= app.project.numItems; i++) {
            var item = app.project.item(i);
            if (item instanceof CompItem)
              comps.push({
                index: i,
                id: item.id,
                name: item.name,
                width: item.width,
                height: item.height,
                duration: item.duration,
                frameRate: item.frameRate,
                numLayers: item.numLayers,
              });
          }
          return { comps: comps };
        case "getActiveComp":
          var comp = app.project ? app.project.activeItem : null;
          if (!comp || !(comp instanceof CompItem))
            return { error: "No active composition" };
          return {
            index: comp.itemIndex,
            id: comp.id,
            name: comp.name,
            width: comp.width,
            height: comp.height,
            duration: comp.duration,
            frameRate: comp.frameRate,
            numLayers: comp.numLayers,
            time: comp.time,
          };
        case "setActiveComp":
          var comp = null;
          for (var k = 1; k <= app.project.numItems; k++) {
            var ci = app.project.item(k);
            if (ci instanceof CompItem && ci.id == cmd.id) {
              comp = ci;
              break;
            }
          }
          if (!comp) return { error: "Not found" };
          comp.openInViewer();
          return { success: true, name: comp.name };
        case "setCompSettings":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Comp Settings");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition" };
            }
            if (cmd.width !== undefined && cmd.width > 0)
              comp.width = Math.round(cmd.width);
            if (cmd.height !== undefined && cmd.height > 0)
              comp.height = Math.round(cmd.height);
            if (cmd.frameRate !== undefined && cmd.frameRate > 0)
              comp.frameRate = cmd.frameRate;
            if (cmd.duration !== undefined && cmd.duration > 0)
              comp.duration = cmd.duration;
            if (cmd.bgColor) comp.bgColor = cmd.bgColor;
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return {
              success: true,
              width: comp.width,
              height: comp.height,
              frameRate: comp.frameRate,
              duration: comp.duration,
            };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "getCompSettings":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          return {
            width: comp.width,
            height: comp.height,
            frameRate: comp.frameRate,
            duration: comp.duration,
            bgColor: $.global._aeHubSV(comp.bgColor),
            motionBlur: comp.motionBlur,
            name: comp.name,
          };
        case "setMotionBlur":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          comp.motionBlur = cmd.enabled;
          return { success: true, motionBlur: comp.motionBlur };

        case "getLayers":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          var layers = [];
          for (var i = 1; i <= comp.numLayers; i++) {
            var l = comp.layer(i);
            layers.push({
              index: i,
              name: l.name,
              enabled: l.enabled,
              locked: l.locked,
              solo: l.solo,
              shy: l.shy,
              threeDLayer: l.threeDLayer,
              hasVideo: l.hasVideo,
              hasAudio: l.hasAudio,
              audioEnabled: l.audioEnabled,
              startTime: l.startTime,
              inPoint: l.inPoint,
              outPoint: l.outPoint,
              layerType: $.global._aeHubGLT(l),
              selected: l.selected,
              parentIndex: l.parent ? l.parent.index : null,
              stretch: l.stretch,
            });
          }
          return {
            layers: layers,
            compName: comp.name,
            compTime: comp.time,
            compDuration: comp.duration,
            compFps: comp.frameRate,
          };
        case "selectLayer":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          if (!cmd.addSelection) {
            for (var i = 1; i <= comp.numLayers; i++)
              comp.layer(i).selected = false;
          }
          if (
            cmd.layerIndex &&
            cmd.layerIndex >= 1 &&
            cmd.layerIndex <= comp.numLayers
          )
            comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex).selected = !comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex)
              .selected;
          if (cmd.index && cmd.index >= 1 && cmd.index <= comp.numLayers)
            comp.layer(cmd.index).selected = !comp.layer(cmd.index).selected;
          return { success: true };
        case "getLayerProperties":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          var layer = comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex || cmd.index);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          return {
            properties: $.global._aeHubGPT(layer),
            layerName: layer.name,
            layerType: $.global._aeHubGLT(layer),
            blendMode: layer.blendingMode.toString(),
            parentIndex: layer.parent ? layer.parent.index : null,
            stretch: layer.stretch,
            threeDLayer: layer.threeDLayer,
          };
        case "toggleVisibility":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.enabled = !layer.enabled;
          return { success: true };
        case "toggleLock":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.locked = !layer.locked;
          return { success: true };
        case "toggleSolo":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.solo = !layer.solo;
          return { success: true };
        case "setLayerProperty":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          switch (cmd.property) {
            case "name":
              layer.name = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "enabled":
              layer.enabled = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "audioEnabled":
              layer.audioEnabled = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "locked":
              layer.locked = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "solo":
              layer.solo = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "shy":
              layer.shy = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "startTime":
              layer.startTime = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "inPoint":
              layer.inPoint = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "outPoint":
              layer.outPoint = cmd.value;
              break;
            case "threeDLayer":
              layer.threeDLayer = cmd.value;
              break;
            default:
              return { error: "Unknown: " + cmd.property };
          }
          return { success: true };
        case "duplicateLayer":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var dup = layer.duplicate();
          return { success: true, layerIndex: dup.index, name: dup.name };
        case "deleteLayer":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.remove();
          return { success: true };
        case "reorderLayer":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
          comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex).moveTo(cmd.toIndex);
          return { success: true };
        case "splitLayer":
          try {
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) return { error: "No active composition" };
            var layer = comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
            if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
            var ct = comp.time;
            if (ct <= layer.inPoint || ct >= layer.outPoint)
              return { error: "Playhead must be within layer" };
            app.beginUndoGroup("AEHub Split");
            var nl = layer.duplicate();
            layer.outPoint = ct;
            nl.inPoint = ct;
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return {
              success: true,
              newLayerIndex: nl.index,
              newLayerName: nl.name,
            };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }

        case "getProperty":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          return $.global._aeHubGPI(prop);
        case "setValue":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          if (cmd.autoKey && prop.numKeys > 0) {
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (comp) prop.setValueAtTime(comp.time, cmd.value);
            else prop.setValue(cmd.value);
          } else prop.setValue(cmd.value);
          return { success: true, newValue: $.global._aeHubSV(prop.value) };
        case "setValueAtTime":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          prop.setValueAtTime(cmd.time, cmd.value);
          return { success: true };

        case "setKeyframe":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          var time = cmd.time !== undefined ? cmd.time : comp.time;
          if (cmd.value !== undefined) prop.setValueAtTime(time, cmd.value);
          else prop.setValueAtTime(time, prop.value);
          return { success: true, numKeys: prop.numKeys };
        case "removeKeyframeAtTime":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop || !prop.isTimeVarying) return { error: "No keyframes" };
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          var time = cmd.time !== undefined ? cmd.time : comp.time;
          var ki = prop.nearestKeyIndex(time);
          if (Math.abs(prop.keyTime(ki) - time) < 1 / comp.frameRate) {
            prop.removeKey(ki);
            return { success: true, numKeys: prop.numKeys };
          }
          return { error: "No keyframe at this time" };
        case "getKeyframes":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          if (!prop.isTimeVarying)
            return { keyframes: [], isTimeVarying: false };
          var keys = [];
          for (var i = 1; i <= prop.numKeys; i++)
            keys.push({
              index: i,
              time: prop.keyTime(i),
              value: $.global._aeHubSV(prop.keyValue(i)),
            });
          return {
            keyframes: keys,
            isTimeVarying: true,
            numKeys: prop.numKeys,
          };

        case "setExpression":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          prop.expression = cmd.expression || "";
          return { success: true };
        case "getExpression":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          return {
            expression: prop.expression,
            expressionEnabled: prop.expressionEnabled,
          };
        case "setLoopExpression":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var prop = $.global._aeHubGBP(layer, cmd.propertyPath);
          if (!prop) return { error: "Not found" };
          if (!cmd.mode || cmd.mode === "off") prop.expression = "";
          else if (cmd.mode === "cycle") prop.expression = "loopOut('cycle');";
          else if (cmd.mode === "pingpong")
            prop.expression = "loopOut('pingpong');";
          else if (cmd.mode === "offset")
            prop.expression = "loopOut('offset');";
          return { success: true, expression: prop.expression };

        case "getEffectsList":
          return { effects: $.global._aeHubGCE() };
        case "addEffect":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var fx = layer
            .property("ADBE Effect Parade")
            .addProperty(cmd.effectMatchName);
          if (!fx) return { error: "Could not add" };
          return {
            success: true,
            effectName: fx.name,
            matchName: fx.matchName,
            index: fx.propertyIndex,
          };
        case "removeEffect":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var fx = layer
            .property("ADBE Effect Parade")
            .property(cmd.effectIndex);
          if (!fx) return { error: "Not found" };
          fx.remove();
          return { success: true };
        case "getEffectProperties":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var fx = layer
            .property("ADBE Effect Parade")
            .property(cmd.effectIndex);
          if (!fx) return { error: "Not found" };
          return { effectName: fx.name, properties: $.global._aeHubGPT(fx) };

        case "addShapeRectangle":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var contents = layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");
          var target = cmd.groupIndex
            ? contents.property(cmd.groupIndex).property("ADBE Vectors Group")
            : contents;
          var grp = target.addProperty("ADBE Vector Group");
          grp.name = cmd.name || "Rectangle";
          var vg = grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");
          var rect = vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Shape - Rect");
          if (cmd.size)
            rect.property("ADBE Vector Rect Size").setValue(cmd.size);
          if (cmd.roundness !== undefined)
            rect.property("ADBE Vector Rect Roundness").setValue(cmd.roundness);
          var fill = vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Fill");
          if (cmd.fillColor)
            fill.property("ADBE Vector Fill Color").setValue(cmd.fillColor);
          return { success: true, groupIndex: grp.propertyIndex };
        case "addShapeEllipse":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var contents = layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");
          var target = cmd.groupIndex
            ? contents.property(cmd.groupIndex).property("ADBE Vectors Group")
            : contents;
          var grp = target.addProperty("ADBE Vector Group");
          grp.name = cmd.name || "Ellipse";
          var vg = grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");
          var ell = vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Shape - Ellipse");
          if (cmd.size) ell.property("ADBE Ellipse Size").setValue(cmd.size);
          var fill = vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Fill");
          if (cmd.fillColor)
            fill.property("ADBE Vector Fill Color").setValue(cmd.fillColor);
          return { success: true, groupIndex: grp.propertyIndex };
        case "addStroke":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var contents = layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");
          var grp = contents.property(cmd.groupIndex);
          if (!grp) return { error: "Not found" };
          var vg = grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");
          var stroke = vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Stroke");
          if (cmd.color)
            stroke.property("ADBE Vector Stroke Color").setValue(cmd.color);
          if (cmd.width !== undefined)
            stroke.property("ADBE Vector Stroke Width").setValue(cmd.width);
          return { success: true };

        case "createSolid":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Solid");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var s = comp.layers.addSolid(
              cmd.color || [1, 1, 1],
              cmd.name || "Solid",
              cmd.width || comp.width || 1920,
              cmd.height || comp.height || 1080,
              1,
              cmd.duration || comp.duration || 10,
            );
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: s.index, name: s.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "createText":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Text");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var t = comp.layers.addText(cmd.text || "Text");
            if (cmd.name) t.name = cmd.name;
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: t.index, name: t.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "createShape":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Shape");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var sl = comp.layers.addShape();
            if (cmd.name) sl.name = cmd.name;
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: sl.index, name: sl.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "createNull":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Null");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var n = comp.layers.addNull(cmd.duration || comp.duration || 10);
            if (cmd.name) n.name = cmd.name;
            if (cmd.threeD) n.threeDLayer = true;
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: n.index, name: n.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "createCamera":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Camera");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var cw = comp.width || 1920;
            var ch = comp.height || 1080;
            var c = comp.layers.addCamera(
              cmd.name || "Camera",
              cmd.center || [cw / 2, ch / 2],
            );
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: c.index, name: c.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        case "createLight":
          try {
            app.beginUndoGroup("Create Light");
            var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
            if (!comp) {
              app.endUndoGroup();
              return { error: "No active composition found." };
            }
            var cw = comp.width || 1920;
            var ch = comp.height || 1080;
            var lt = comp.layers.addLight(
              cmd.name || "Light",
              cmd.center || [cw / 2, ch / 2],
            );
            app.endUndoGroup();
            return { success: true, layerIndex: lt.index, name: lt.name };
          } catch (e) {
            try {
              app.endUndoGroup();
            } catch (e2) {}
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }

        case "addMask":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var mask = layer
            .property("ADBE Mask Parade")
            .addProperty("ADBE Mask Atom");
          if (cmd.name) mask.name = cmd.name;
          if (cmd.shape) mask.property("ADBE Mask Shape").setValue(cmd.shape);
          return { success: true, maskIndex: mask.propertyIndex };
        case "getMasks":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var masks = [];
          var mp = layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade");
          for (var i = 1; i <= mp.numProperties; i++) {
            var m = mp.property(i);
            masks.push({
              index: i,
              name: m.name,
              maskMode: m.property("ADBE Mask Mode").value.toString(),
              inverted: m.property("ADBE Mask Inverted").value,
              maskFeather: $.global._aeHubSV(
                m.property("ADBE Mask Feather").value,
              ),
              maskOpacity: m.property("ADBE Mask Opacity").value,
              maskExpansion: m.property("ADBE Mask Expansion").value,
            });
          }
          return { masks: masks };
        case "setMaskMode":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var mask = layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade").property(cmd.maskIndex);
          if (!mask) return { error: "Mask not found" };
          var mm = {
            Add: MaskMode.ADD,
            Subtract: MaskMode.SUBTRACT,
            Intersect: MaskMode.INTERSECT,
            Lighten: MaskMode.LIGHTEN,
            Darken: MaskMode.DARKEN,
            Difference: MaskMode.DIFFERENCE,
            None: MaskMode.NONE,
          };
          mask.maskMode = mm[cmd.mode] || MaskMode.ADD;
          return { success: true };
        case "setMaskProperty":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var mask = layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade").property(cmd.maskIndex);
          if (!mask) return { error: "Mask not found" };
          if (cmd.feather !== undefined)
            mask.property("ADBE Mask Feather").setValue(cmd.feather);
          if (cmd.opacity !== undefined)
            mask.property("ADBE Mask Opacity").setValue(cmd.opacity);
          if (cmd.expansion !== undefined)
            mask.property("ADBE Mask Expansion").setValue(cmd.expansion);
          if (cmd.inverted !== undefined)
            mask.property("ADBE Mask Inverted").setValue(cmd.inverted);
          return { success: true };

        case "setBlendMode":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          var mm = {
            Normal: BlendingMode.NORMAL,
            Dissolve: BlendingMode.DISSOLVE,
            "Dancing Dissolve": BlendingMode.DANCING_DISSOLVE,
            Darken: BlendingMode.DARKEN,
            Multiply: BlendingMode.MULTIPLY,
            "Color Burn": BlendingMode.COLOR_BURN,
            "Linear Burn": BlendingMode.LINEAR_BURN,
            "Darker Color": BlendingMode.DARKER_COLOR,
            Lighten: BlendingMode.LIGHTEN,
            Screen: BlendingMode.SCREEN,
            "Color Dodge": BlendingMode.COLOR_DODGE,
            "Linear Dodge": BlendingMode.LINEAR_DODGE,
            "Lighter Color": BlendingMode.LIGHTER_COLOR,
            Overlay: BlendingMode.OVERLAY,
            "Soft Light": BlendingMode.SOFT_LIGHT,
            "Hard Light": BlendingMode.HARD_LIGHT,
            "Linear Light": BlendingMode.LINEAR_LIGHT,
            "Vivid Light": BlendingMode.VIVID_LIGHT,
            "Pin Light": BlendingMode.PIN_LIGHT,
            "Hard Mix": BlendingMode.HARD_MIX,
            Difference: BlendingMode.DIFFERENCE,
            Exclusion: BlendingMode.EXCLUSION,
            Subtract: BlendingMode.SUBTRACT,
            Divide: BlendingMode.DIVIDE,
          };
          layer.blendingMode = mm[cmd.mode] || BlendingMode.NORMAL;
          return { success: true, blendMode: layer.blendingMode.toString() };
        case "setParent":
          var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
          if (!comp) return { error: "No comp" };
          var layer = comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          if (!cmd.parentIndex || cmd.parentIndex === 0) layer.parent = null;
          else layer.parent = comp.layer(cmd.parentIndex);
          return { success: true };
        case "setTimeStretch":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.stretch = cmd.stretch;
          return { success: true, stretch: layer.stretch };
        case "reverseLayer":
          var layer = $.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);
          if (!layer) return { error: "Layer not found" };
          layer.stretch = layer.stretch * -1;
          return { success: true, stretch: layer.stretch };
        case "groupLayers": // Pre-compose shortcut
          app.executeCommand(236);
          return { success: true };

        case "undo":
          app.executeCommand(app.findMenuCommandId("Undo") || 16);
          return { success: true };
        case "redo":
          var redoStrs = [
            "Redo",
            "Redo ",
            "Redo Action",
            "Redo Add Layer",
            "Redo Change Value",
          ];
          var rId = 0;
          function findRedo() {
            var base = app.findMenuCommandId("Redo");
            if (base) return base;
            for (var i = 17; i < 4000; i++) {
              try {
                var name = app.findMenuCommandId(i);
              } catch (ev) {}
            }
            return 17;
          }
          var cId = app.findMenuCommandId("Redo") || 17; // 17 is typically redo in many older CC versions
          try {
            app.executeCommand(cId);
          } catch (ex) {}
          return { success: true };
        case "beginUndoGroup":
          app.beginUndoGroup(cmd.name || "AEHub");
          return { success: true };
        case "endUndoGroup":
          app.endUndoGroup();
          return { success: true };
        case "executeScript":
          try {
            var fn = new Function(cmd.script);
            var result = fn();
            return {
              result: result !== undefined ? String(result) : "undefined",
            };
          } catch (e) {
            return { error: e.toString() };
          }
        default:
          return { error: "Unknown: " + cmd.action };
      }
    };

    $.global._aeHubGetComp = function (idx) {
      if (!app.project || !idx) return null;
      var item = app.project.item(idx);
      return item instanceof CompItem ? item : null;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp = function (idx) {
      if (idx) return $.global._aeHubGetComp(idx);
      var comp = app.project ? app.project.activeItem : null;
      return comp instanceof CompItem ? comp : null;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGetLayer = function (cmd) {
      var comp = $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);
      var lId = cmd.layerIndex || cmd.index || cmd.idx;
      if (!comp || !lId) return null;
      return comp.layer(lId);
    };
    $.global._aeHubGLT = function (layer) {
      if (layer instanceof CameraLayer) return "camera";
      if (layer instanceof LightLayer) return "light";
      if (layer instanceof TextLayer) return "text";
      if (layer instanceof ShapeLayer) return "shape";
      if (layer instanceof AVLayer) {
        if (layer.nullLayer) return "null";
        if (layer.source instanceof CompItem) return "comp";
        return "av";
      }
      return "unknown";
    };
    $.global._aeHubSV = function (val) {
      if (val === null || val === undefined) return null;
      if (val instanceof Array) {
        var arr = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < val.length; i++) arr.push(val[i]);
        return arr;
      }
      return val;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGPT = function (parent) {
      var props = [];
      var num = 0;
      try {
        num = parent.numProperties;
      } catch (e) {
        return props;
      }
      for (var i = 1; i <= num; i++) {
        var prop = parent.property(i);
        var info = {
          index: i,
          name: prop.name,
          matchName: prop.matchName,
          propertyType: prop.propertyType,
          isGroup: false,
        };
        try {
          info.isGroup =
            prop.propertyType === PropertyType.INDEXED_GROUP ||
            prop.propertyType === PropertyType.NAMED_GROUP;
        } catch (e) {}
        if (info.isGroup) {
          info.properties = $.global._aeHubGPT(prop);
        } else {
          try {
            info.value = $.global._aeHubSV(prop.value);
          } catch (e) {
            info.value = null;
            info.error = e.toString();
          }
          try {
            info.isTimeVarying = prop.isTimeVarying;
            info.numKeys = prop.isTimeVarying ? prop.numKeys : 0;
            info.canSetExpression = prop.canSetExpression;
            info.propertyValueType = prop.propertyValueType;
            if (info.numKeys > 0) {
              info.keys = [];
              for (var kf = 1; kf <= info.numKeys; kf++) {
                try {
                  info.keys.push(prop.keyTime(kf));
                } catch (ekf) {}
              }
            }
          } catch (e) {}
        }
        props.push(info);
      }
      return props;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGPI = function (prop) {
      var info = { name: prop.name, matchName: prop.matchName };
      try {
        info.value = $.global._aeHubSV(prop.value);
      } catch (e) {
        info.value = null;
      }
      try {
        info.isTimeVarying = prop.isTimeVarying;
      } catch (e) {}
      try {
        info.numKeys = prop.isTimeVarying ? prop.numKeys : 0;
      } catch (e) {}
      try {
        info.expression = prop.expression;
      } catch (e) {}
      try {
        info.expressionEnabled = prop.expressionEnabled;
      } catch (e) {}
      return info;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGBP = function (layer, pathStr) {
      if (!pathStr) return null;
      var parts = pathStr.split("/");
      var current = layer;
      for (var i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
        if (!current || !current.property) return null;
        current = current.property(parts[i]);
      }
      return current;
    };
    $.global._aeHubGCE = function () {
      return [
        { name: "Gaussian Blur", matchName: "ADBE Gaussian Blur 2" },
        {
          name: "Brightness & Contrast",
          matchName: "ADBE Brightness & Contrast 2",
        },
        { name: "Hue/Saturation", matchName: "ADBE HUE SATURATION" },
        { name: "Levels", matchName: "ADBE Levels2" },
        { name: "Curves", matchName: "ADBE CurvesCustom" },
        { name: "Color Balance", matchName: "ADBE Color Balance" },
        { name: "Tint", matchName: "ADBE Tint" },
        { name: "Fill", matchName: "ADBE Fill" },
        { name: "Ramp", matchName: "ADBE Ramp" },
        { name: "Drop Shadow", matchName: "ADBE Drop Shadow" },
        { name: "Glow", matchName: "ADBE Glow 2" },
        { name: "Lightning", matchName: "ADBE Lightning 2" },
        { name: "Lens Flare", matchName: "ADBE Lens Flare" },
        { name: "Fractal Noise", matchName: "ADBE Turbulent Noise" },
        { name: "Shatter", matchName: "ADBE Shatter" },
        { name: "Wave Warp", matchName: "ADBE Wave Warp" },
        { name: "Spherize", matchName: "ADBE Spherize" },
        { name: "Twirl", matchName: "ADBE Twirl" },
        { name: "Displacement Map", matchName: "ADBE Displacement Map" },
        { name: "Corner Pin", matchName: "ADBE Corner Pin" },
        { name: "Motion Tile", matchName: "ADBE Motion Tile" },
        { name: "Echo", matchName: "ADBE Echo" },
        { name: "Posterize Time", matchName: "ADBE Posterize Time" },
        { name: "Sharpen", matchName: "ADBE Sharpen" },
        { name: "Unsharp mask", matchName: "ADBE Unsharp Mask" },
        { name: "Minimax", matchName: "ADBE Minimax" },
        { name: "Find Edges", matchName: "ADBE Find Edges" },
        { name: "Cartoon", matchName: "ADBE Cartoon" },
        { name: "Noise", matchName: "ADBE Noise" },
        { name: "Mosaic", matchName: "ADBE Mosaic" },
        { name: "Transform", matchName: "ADBE Geometry2" },
        { name: "Camera Lens Blur", matchName: "ADBE Camera Lens Blur" },
        { name: "Lumetri Color", matchName: "ADBE Lumetri" },
        { name: "Keylight 1.2", matchName: "Keylight" },
        { name: "3D Camera Tracker", matchName: "ADBE 3D Camera Tracker" },
        { name: "Warp Stabilizer", matchName: "ADBE Mocha" },
      ];
    };

    app.scheduleTask("_aeHubPoll()", 100, false);
    app.scheduleTask("_aeHubSync()", 1000, false);
  } else {
    alert("AE Control Hub: Cannot connect.\nMake sure server is running.");
  }
})();

FILE: diagnose.js
------------------------------------------------------------

const WebSocket = require('ws');

console.log("Starting AE Bridge diagnostics...");
console.log("Attempting to connect to WS on port 3000...");

const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:3000');

ws.on('open', () => {
    console.log("-----------------------------------------");
    console.log("[DIAGNOSE] Connected to TouchTools server");
    console.log("-----------------------------------------");
    
    // 1. Send Ping
    console.log("[DIAGNOSE] Sending Ping to test connection...");
    ws.send(JSON.stringify({
        action: "sendToAE",
        command: { reqId: "ping_1", action: "ping" }
    }));

    // 2. Request getActiveComp
    console.log("[DIAGNOSE] Asking AE for active composition...");
    ws.send(JSON.stringify({
        action: "sendToAE",
        command: { reqId: "comp_1", action: "getActiveComp" }
    }));

    // 3. Try creating a null layer
    setTimeout(() => {
        console.log("[DIAGNOSE] Try creating a Null Layer to catch errors...");
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({
            action: "sendToAE",
            command: { reqId: "null_1", action: "createNull", name: "DiagTestNull" }
        }));
    }, 1000);

    // Timeout
    setTimeout(() => {
        console.log("-----------------------------------------");
        console.log("[DIAGNOSE] Finishing test and exiting.");
        process.exit();
    }, 4000);
});

ws.on('message', (data) => {
    try {
        const msg = JSON.parse(data);
        if (msg.type === "bridge_status") {
            console.log(`[Bridge Status] Active: ${msg.connected}`);
        } else if (msg.type === "result") {
            console.log(`\n✅ [SUCCESS] Result for ${msg.reqId}:`, JSON.stringify(msg.data, null, 2));
        } else if (msg.type === "error") {
            console.log(`\n❌ [ERROR] from AE for ${msg.reqId}: ${msg.error}`);
            console.log("If an error occurred, this is likely what is breaking the UI actions.");
        } else {
            // Probably status updates
            if (msg.message === "sync") {
                // ignoring noisy sync
            } else {
                console.log("[Notice] Other message:", data.toString());
            }
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.log("Raw Msg:", data.toString());
    }
});

ws.on('error', (err) => {
    console.error("[DIAGNOSE] WebSocket Error:", err.message);
    if(err.message.includes("ECONNREFUSED")) {
        console.log("Make sure npm run dev is running on port 3000!");
    }
});

FILE: direction.md
------------------------------------------------------------

# Touch Tools for After Effects - Project Requirements & Journey

## 1. Core Vision & Purpose
My primary goal was to build "Touch Tools," a web-based, touch-friendly companion application for Adobe After Effects. It acts as a remote control surface, allowing me to manipulate AE compositions, layers, and properties fluidly using a modern web interface on a tablet or touchscreen. The app connects to AE via WebSockets and an ExtendScript (`bridge.jsx`) backend.

## 2. UI/UX Design Requirements
From the beginning, I wanted a highly polished, technical, and dark-themed interface specifically designed for touch interaction.
* **Aesthetic:** Dark mode, high contrast, using a custom color palette (`tt-bg`, `tt-surface`, `tt-warning`, `tt-accent`). Needed to feel like a pro-tool, not a generic website.
* **Touch-First Controls:** Standard inputs don't work well for touch. I specifically needed:
  * **ScrubDials:** For sliding/dragging to change values rather than just typing them. They needed to handle sensitivity, steps, and units (px, %, °, etc.).
  * **Trackpads:** For 2D and 3D spatial properties (Position, Anchor point) to manipulate X and Y simultaneously.
* **Layout & Navigation:** 
  * A main composition timeline view.
  * An Action Sheet (bottom drawer/overlay) for layer specific options rather than deep, clunky routing.
  * Fluid animations between states using `motion/react` (Framer Motion).
  * No empty space or overlapping components—everything needed to fit logically and expansively within the viewport.

## 3. Functional Requirements
The logic needed to perfectly mirror and manipulate the state of the active After Effects project. 
* **Timeline Controls:** Play, pause, seek, and step frame-by-frame.
* **Layer Management:** 
  * List all layers in the active comp.
  * Support for locking, soloing, and toggling visibility.
  * Double-clicking a layer should select it and open its specific properties without jarring UI overlaps.
  * Support for Base Layer Properties like After Effects Blend Modes (Normal, Add, Multiply, etc.) and Time Stretch percentages.
* **Property Manipulation (The Inspector):**
  * Manipulate explicit Transform properties (Anchor Point, Position, Scale, Rotation, Opacity).
  * Auto-detect 3D layers and reveal Z-axis controls. 
  * Dynamically parse and render nested AE property groups (like Effects, Masks, Shapes) in a generic way so any effect could be tweaked.
* **Keyframing:**
  * Direct ability to add and remove keyframes on properties right from the UI (the Scrub Dials).
  * Visual feedback (glowing warning colors, diamond icons) when a property currently has a keyframe at the playhead.

## 4. Key Issues, Iterations, and Fixes
Throughout the development, we refined several core behaviors based on my specific input:

* **Scrub Dial & UI Overlaps:** The Scrub Dials were initially messy, with text overlapping the keyframe buttons. We revised the flexbox layout, enforced `flex-col`, and added a polished diamond keyframe icon (`group-hover/key`) that glows yellow (`drop-shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(255,214,0,0.6)]`) when active.
* **Property Inspector Clutter:** I didn't want duplicate Transform properties showing up if we already had a dedicated panel for them. We implemented logic in `GenericPropertiesPanel` to gracefully handle and filter `ADBE Transform Group` and build out dynamic rendering for multidimensional properties (Arrays like X, Y, Z).
* **Keyframe Precision:** Toggling keyframes was initially imprecise. We revised the ExtendScript injected via sockets to use `nearestKeyIndex` and threshold time checks (`Math.abs(p.keyTime(ki) - c.time) < 0.05`) so that pressing the keyframe button exactly adds or removes the keyframe on that specific frame without throwing errors.
* **Navigation Flow (Double Click Bug):** Double-clicking a layer was triggering the Action Sheet aggressively and causing visual overlaps. We modified the `handleLayerDoubleClick` to only select the layer and delegate the view state, allowing the layout to remain clean.
* **Blend Modes & Base Properties:** I required standard AE Blend modes and Time Stretch to be easily accessible from the properties panel without needing to script custom AE commands manually every time.

## 5. Deployment / Architecture Rules
* Keep the connection real-time via `socket.io`.
* Ensure `bridge.jsx` is robust enough to not crash AE (using try-catch blocks and active item validations).
* Let `server.ts` act as the middleman between the React frontend and After Effects.

(function(){
try{if($.global._aeHubSocket)$.global._aeHubSocket.close()}catch(e){}

$.global._aeHubSafeWrite=function(str){
    var clean=str.replace(/[\r\n]/g,"");
    var max=4000;
    for(var i=0;i<clean.length;i+=max){$.global._aeHubSocket.write(clean.substring(i,i+max))}
    $.global._aeHubSocket.write("\n");
};

$.global._aeHubSocket=new Socket();
$.global._aeHubBuffer="";
$.global._aeHubConnected=false;

try{$.global._aeHubConnected=$.global._aeHubSocket.open("127.0.0.1:8092","utf-8")}catch(e){$.global._aeHubConnected=false}

if($.global._aeHubConnected){
    $.global._aeHubSocket.timeout=0;
    $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(JSON.stringify({type:"status",message:"bridge_connected"}));

    $.global._aeHubPoll=function(){
        if(!$.global._aeHubConnected)return;
        try{
            var data=$.global._aeHubSocket.read();
            if(data&&data.length>0){
                $.global._aeHubBuffer+=data;
                var lines=$.global._aeHubBuffer.split("\n");
                $.global._aeHubBuffer=lines.pop();
                for(var i=0;i<lines.length;i++){
                    var line=lines[i].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
                    if(!line)continue;
                    try{
                        var cmd=JSON.parse(line);
                        var result=$.global._aeHubExec(cmd);
                        $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(JSON.stringify({type:"result",reqId:cmd.reqId,data:result}));
                    }catch(e){
                        try{if(typeof cmd!=='undefined') $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(JSON.stringify({type:"error",reqId:cmd.reqId,error:e.toString()}))}catch(e2){}
                    }
                }
            }
        }catch(e){$.global._aeHubConnected=false;return}
        app.scheduleTask("_aeHubPoll()",50,false);
    };

    $.global._aeHubSync = function() {
        if (!$.global._aeHubConnected) return;
        try {
            var activeComp = null;
            var comp = app.project ? app.project.activeItem : null;
            var comps = [];
            var layers = [];

            if (app.project) {
                for (var i = 1; i <= app.project.numItems; i++) {
                    var item = app.project.item(i);
                    if (item instanceof CompItem) comps.push({id: item.id, name: item.name});
                }
            }

            if (comp && comp instanceof CompItem) {
                activeComp = { index: comp.itemIndex, id: comp.id, name: comp.name, width: comp.width, height: comp.height, duration: comp.duration, frameRate: comp.frameRate, numLayers: comp.numLayers, time: comp.time };
                for (var j = 1; j <= Math.min(comp.numLayers, 50); j++) {
                    var l = comp.layer(j);
                    layers.push({
                        index: j,
                        name: l.name,
                        selected: l.selected,
                        enabled: l.enabled,
                        locked: l.locked,
                        hasVideo: l.hasVideo,
                        hasAudio: l.hasAudio,
                        audioEnabled: l.audioEnabled,
                        solo: l.solo,
                        type: $.global._aeHubGLT(l)
                    });
                }
            }

            $.global._aeHubSafeWrite(JSON.stringify({
                type: "status",
                message: "sync",
                state: { activeComp: activeComp, layers: layers, compositions: comps }
            }));
        } catch(e) {}
        app.scheduleTask("_aeHubSync()", 1000, false);
    };

    $.global._aeHubExec=function(cmd){
        switch(cmd.action){
        case"ping":return{pong:true,time:new Date().toString()};
        case"getAppInfo":return{appName:app.appName,version:app.version,buildNumber:app.buildNumber,language:app.language,projectFile:app.project&&app.project.file?app.project.file.fsName:null,projectName:app.project?app.project.name:null};
        case"playPause":
            try { app.executeCommand(1045); } catch(e) {
                try { app.executeCommand(app.findMenuCommandId("Preview")); } catch(e2) {}
            }
            return{success:true};

        case"getComps":
            var comps=[];
            if(!app.project)return{comps:comps};
            for(var i=1;i<=app.project.numItems;i++){var item=app.project.item(i);if(item instanceof CompItem)comps.push({index:i,id:item.id,name:item.name,width:item.width,height:item.height,duration:item.duration,frameRate:item.frameRate,numLayers:item.numLayers})}
            return{comps:comps};
        case"getActiveComp":
            var comp=app.project?app.project.activeItem:null;
            if(!comp||!(comp instanceof CompItem))return{error:"No active composition"};
            return{index:comp.itemIndex,id:comp.id,name:comp.name,width:comp.width,height:comp.height,duration:comp.duration,frameRate:comp.frameRate,numLayers:comp.numLayers,time:comp.time};
        case"setActiveComp":
            var comp=null;
            for(var k=1;k<=app.project.numItems;k++){var ci=app.project.item(k);if(ci instanceof CompItem && ci.id == cmd.id){comp=ci;break;}}
            if(!comp)return{error:"Not found"};comp.openInViewer();return{success:true,name:comp.name};
        case"setCompSettings":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
            if(cmd.width!==undefined)comp.width=cmd.width;if(cmd.height!==undefined)comp.height=cmd.height;
            if(cmd.frameRate!==undefined)comp.frameRate=cmd.frameRate;if(cmd.duration!==undefined)comp.duration=cmd.duration;
            if(cmd.bgColor)comp.bgColor=cmd.bgColor;
            return{success:true,width:comp.width,height:comp.height,frameRate:comp.frameRate,duration:comp.duration};
        case"getCompSettings":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
            return{width:comp.width,height:comp.height,frameRate:comp.frameRate,duration:comp.duration,bgColor:$.global._aeHubSV(comp.bgColor),motionBlur:comp.motionBlur,name:comp.name};
        case"setMotionBlur":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};comp.motionBlur=cmd.enabled;return{success:true,motionBlur:comp.motionBlur};

        case"getLayers":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
            var layers=[];
            for(var i=1;i<=comp.numLayers;i++){
                var l=comp.layer(i);
                layers.push({index:i,name:l.name,enabled:l.enabled,locked:l.locked,solo:l.solo,shy:l.shy,threeDLayer:l.threeDLayer,hasVideo:l.hasVideo,hasAudio:l.hasAudio,audioEnabled:l.audioEnabled,startTime:l.startTime,inPoint:l.inPoint,outPoint:l.outPoint,layerType:$.global._aeHubGLT(l),selected:l.selected,parentIndex:l.parent?l.parent.index:null,stretch:l.stretch});
            }
            return{layers:layers,compName:comp.name,compTime:comp.time,compDuration:comp.duration,compFps:comp.frameRate};
        case"selectLayer":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
            for(var i=1;i<=comp.numLayers;i++)comp.layer(i).selected=false;
            if(cmd.layerIndex&&cmd.layerIndex>=1&&cmd.layerIndex<=comp.numLayers)comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex).selected=true;
            if(cmd.index&&cmd.index>=1&&cmd.index<=comp.numLayers)comp.layer(cmd.index).selected=true; // Added cmd.index fallback
            return{success:true};
        case"getLayerProperties":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
            var layer=comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex || cmd.index);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            return{properties:$.global._aeHubGPT(layer),layerName:layer.name,layerType:$.global._aeHubGLT(layer),blendMode:layer.blendingMode.toString(),parentIndex:layer.parent?layer.parent.index:null,stretch:layer.stretch,threeDLayer:layer.threeDLayer};
        case"toggleVisibility":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"}; layer.enabled = !layer.enabled; return{success:true};
        case"toggleLock":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"}; layer.locked = !layer.locked; return{success:true};
        case"toggleSolo":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"}; layer.solo = !layer.solo; return{success:true};
        case"setLayerProperty":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            switch(cmd.property){case"name":layer.name=cmd.value;break;case"enabled":layer.enabled=cmd.value;break;case"audioEnabled":layer.audioEnabled=cmd.value;break;case"locked":layer.locked=cmd.value;break;case"solo":layer.solo=cmd.value;break;case"shy":layer.shy=cmd.value;break;case"startTime":layer.startTime=cmd.value;break;case"inPoint":layer.inPoint=cmd.value;break;case"outPoint":layer.outPoint=cmd.value;break;case"threeDLayer":layer.threeDLayer=cmd.value;break;default:return{error:"Unknown: "+cmd.property}}
            return{success:true};
        case"duplicateLayer":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var dup=layer.duplicate();return{success:true,layerIndex:dup.index,name:dup.name};
        case"deleteLayer":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};layer.remove();return{success:true};
        case"reorderLayer":var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex).moveTo(cmd.toIndex);return{success:true};
        case"splitLayer":
            try {
                var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No active composition"};
                var layer=comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
                var ct=comp.time;if(ct<=layer.inPoint||ct>=layer.outPoint)return{error:"Playhead must be within layer"};
                app.beginUndoGroup("AEHub Split");var nl=layer.duplicate();layer.outPoint=ct;nl.inPoint=ct;app.endUndoGroup();
                return{success:true,newLayerIndex:nl.index,newLayerName:nl.name};
            } catch(e) {
                try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};
            }

        case"getProperty":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};return $.global._aeHubGPI(prop);
        case"setValue":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};
            if(cmd.autoKey&&prop.numKeys>0){var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(comp)prop.setValueAtTime(comp.time,cmd.value);else prop.setValue(cmd.value)}
            else prop.setValue(cmd.value);
            return{success:true,newValue:$.global._aeHubSV(prop.value)};
        case"setValueAtTime":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};prop.setValueAtTime(cmd.time,cmd.value);return{success:true};

        case"setKeyframe":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};
            var time=cmd.time!==undefined?cmd.time:comp.time;
            if(cmd.value!==undefined)prop.setValueAtTime(time,cmd.value);else prop.setValueAtTime(time,prop.value);
            return{success:true,numKeys:prop.numKeys};
        case"removeKeyframeAtTime":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop||!prop.isTimeVarying)return{error:"No keyframes"};
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);var time=cmd.time!==undefined?cmd.time:comp.time;
            var ki=prop.nearestKeyIndex(time);
            if(Math.abs(prop.keyTime(ki)-time)<1/comp.frameRate){prop.removeKey(ki);return{success:true,numKeys:prop.numKeys}}
            return{error:"No keyframe at this time"};
        case"getKeyframes":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};
            if(!prop.isTimeVarying)return{keyframes:[],isTimeVarying:false};
            var keys=[];for(var i=1;i<=prop.numKeys;i++)keys.push({index:i,time:prop.keyTime(i),value:$.global._aeHubSV(prop.keyValue(i))});
            return{keyframes:keys,isTimeVarying:true,numKeys:prop.numKeys};

        case"setExpression":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};prop.expression=cmd.expression||"";return{success:true};
        case"getExpression":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};return{expression:prop.expression,expressionEnabled:prop.expressionEnabled};
        case"setLoopExpression":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var prop=$.global._aeHubGBP(layer,cmd.propertyPath);if(!prop)return{error:"Not found"};
            if(!cmd.mode||cmd.mode==="off")prop.expression="";
            else if(cmd.mode==="cycle")prop.expression="loopOut('cycle');";
            else if(cmd.mode==="pingpong")prop.expression="loopOut('pingpong');";
            else if(cmd.mode==="offset")prop.expression="loopOut('offset');";
            return{success:true,expression:prop.expression};

        case"getEffectsList":return{effects:$.global._aeHubGCE()};
        case"addEffect":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var fx=layer.property("ADBE Effect Parade").addProperty(cmd.effectMatchName);if(!fx)return{error:"Could not add"};return{success:true,effectName:fx.name,matchName:fx.matchName,index:fx.propertyIndex};
        case"removeEffect":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var fx=layer.property("ADBE Effect Parade").property(cmd.effectIndex);if(!fx)return{error:"Not found"};fx.remove();return{success:true};
        case"getEffectProperties":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var fx=layer.property("ADBE Effect Parade").property(cmd.effectIndex);if(!fx)return{error:"Not found"};return{effectName:fx.name,properties:$.global._aeHubGPT(fx)};

        case"addShapeRectangle":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var contents=layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");var target=cmd.groupIndex?contents.property(cmd.groupIndex).property("ADBE Vectors Group"):contents;
            var grp=target.addProperty("ADBE Vector Group");grp.name=cmd.name||"Rectangle";
            var vg=grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");var rect=vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Shape - Rect");
            if(cmd.size)rect.property("ADBE Vector Rect Size").setValue(cmd.size);if(cmd.roundness!==undefined)rect.property("ADBE Vector Rect Roundness").setValue(cmd.roundness);
            var fill=vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Fill");if(cmd.fillColor)fill.property("ADBE Vector Fill Color").setValue(cmd.fillColor);
            return{success:true,groupIndex:grp.propertyIndex};
        case"addShapeEllipse":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var contents=layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");var target=cmd.groupIndex?contents.property(cmd.groupIndex).property("ADBE Vectors Group"):contents;
            var grp=target.addProperty("ADBE Vector Group");grp.name=cmd.name||"Ellipse";
            var vg=grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");var ell=vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Shape - Ellipse");
            if(cmd.size)ell.property("ADBE Ellipse Size").setValue(cmd.size);
            var fill=vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Fill");if(cmd.fillColor)fill.property("ADBE Vector Fill Color").setValue(cmd.fillColor);
            return{success:true,groupIndex:grp.propertyIndex};
        case"addStroke":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var contents=layer.property("ADBE Root Vectors Group");var grp=contents.property(cmd.groupIndex);if(!grp)return{error:"Not found"};
            var vg=grp.property("ADBE Vectors Group");var stroke=vg.addProperty("ADBE Vector Graphic - Stroke");
            if(cmd.color)stroke.property("ADBE Vector Stroke Color").setValue(cmd.color);if(cmd.width!==undefined)stroke.property("ADBE Vector Stroke Width").setValue(cmd.width);
            return{success:true};

        case"createSolid":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Solid");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var s=comp.layers.addSolid(cmd.color||[0.1,0.1,0.1],cmd.name||"Solid",cmd.width||comp.width,cmd.height||comp.height,1,cmd.duration||comp.duration);app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:s.index,name:s.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}
        case"createText":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Text");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var t=comp.layers.addText(cmd.text||"Text");if(cmd.name)t.name=cmd.name;app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:t.index,name:t.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}
        case"createShape":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Shape");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var sl=comp.layers.addShape();if(cmd.name)sl.name=cmd.name;app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:sl.index,name:sl.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}
        case"createNull":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Null");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var n=comp.layers.addNull(cmd.duration||comp.duration);if(cmd.name)n.name=cmd.name;if(cmd.threeD)n.threeDLayer=true;app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:n.index,name:n.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}
        case"createCamera":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Camera");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var c=comp.layers.addCamera(cmd.name||"Camera",cmd.center||[comp.width/2,comp.height/2]);app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:c.index,name:c.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}
        case"createLight":try{app.beginUndoGroup("Create Light");var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp){app.endUndoGroup();return{error:"No active composition found."}};var lt=comp.layers.addLight(cmd.name||"Light",cmd.center||[comp.width/2,comp.height/2]);app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true,layerIndex:lt.index,name:lt.name};}catch(e){try{app.endUndoGroup();}catch(e2){}return{error:e.toString()};}

        case"addMask":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};var mask=layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade").addProperty("ADBE Mask Atom");if(cmd.name)mask.name=cmd.name;if(cmd.shape)mask.property("ADBE Mask Shape").setValue(cmd.shape);return{success:true,maskIndex:mask.propertyIndex};
        case"getMasks":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var masks=[];var mp=layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade");
            for(var i=1;i<=mp.numProperties;i++){var m=mp.property(i);masks.push({index:i,name:m.name,maskMode:m.property("ADBE Mask Mode").value.toString(),inverted:m.property("ADBE Mask Inverted").value,maskFeather:$.global._aeHubSV(m.property("ADBE Mask Feather").value),maskOpacity:m.property("ADBE Mask Opacity").value,maskExpansion:m.property("ADBE Mask Expansion").value})}
            return{masks:masks};
        case"setMaskMode":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var mask=layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade").property(cmd.maskIndex);if(!mask)return{error:"Mask not found"};
            var mm={"Add":MaskMode.ADD,"Subtract":MaskMode.SUBTRACT,"Intersect":MaskMode.INTERSECT,"Lighten":MaskMode.LIGHTEN,"Darken":MaskMode.DARKEN,"Difference":MaskMode.DIFFERENCE,"None":MaskMode.NONE};
            mask.maskMode=mm[cmd.mode]||MaskMode.ADD;return{success:true};
        case"setMaskProperty":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var mask=layer.property("ADBE Mask Parade").property(cmd.maskIndex);if(!mask)return{error:"Mask not found"};
            if(cmd.feather!==undefined)mask.property("ADBE Mask Feather").setValue(cmd.feather);
            if(cmd.opacity!==undefined)mask.property("ADBE Mask Opacity").setValue(cmd.opacity);
            if(cmd.expansion!==undefined)mask.property("ADBE Mask Expansion").setValue(cmd.expansion);
            if(cmd.inverted!==undefined)mask.property("ADBE Mask Inverted").setValue(cmd.inverted);
            return{success:true};

        case"setBlendMode":
            var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            var mm={"Normal":BlendingMode.NORMAL,"Multiply":BlendingMode.MULTIPLY,"Screen":BlendingMode.SCREEN,"Overlay":BlendingMode.OVERLAY,"Add":BlendingMode.ADD,"SoftLight":BlendingMode.SOFT_LIGHT,"HardLight":BlendingMode.HARD_LIGHT,"Difference":BlendingMode.DIFFERENCE,"Exclusion":BlendingMode.EXCLUSION,"Darken":BlendingMode.DARKEN,"Lighten":BlendingMode.LIGHTEN,"ColorDodge":BlendingMode.COLOR_DODGE,"ColorBurn":BlendingMode.COLOR_BURN,"Hue":BlendingMode.HUE,"Saturation":BlendingMode.SATURATION,"Color":BlendingMode.COLOR,"Luminosity":BlendingMode.LUMINOSITY};
            layer.blendingMode=mm[cmd.mode]||BlendingMode.NORMAL;return{success:true,blendMode:layer.blendingMode.toString()};
        case"setParent":
            var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);if(!comp)return{error:"No comp"};
            var layer=comp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};
            if(!cmd.parentIndex||cmd.parentIndex===0)layer.parent=null;else layer.parent=comp.layer(cmd.parentIndex);
            return{success:true};
        case"setTimeStretch":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};layer.stretch=cmd.stretch;return{success:true,stretch:layer.stretch};
        case"reverseLayer":var layer=$.global._aeHubGetLayer(cmd);if(!layer)return{error:"Layer not found"};layer.stretch=layer.stretch*-1;return{success:true,stretch:layer.stretch};

        case"undo":app.executeCommand(16);return{success:true};
        case"redo":app.executeCommand(17);return{success:true};
        case"beginUndoGroup":app.beginUndoGroup(cmd.name||"AEHub");return{success:true};
        case"endUndoGroup":app.endUndoGroup();return{success:true};
        case"executeScript":try{var fn=new Function(cmd.script);var result=fn();return{result:result!==undefined?String(result):"undefined"}}catch(e){return{error:e.toString()}};
        default:return{error:"Unknown: "+cmd.action};
        }
    };

    $.global._aeHubGetComp=function(idx){if(!app.project||!idx)return null;var item=app.project.item(idx);return(item instanceof CompItem)?item:null};
    $.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp=function(idx){if(idx)return $.global._aeHubGetComp(idx);var comp=app.project?app.project.activeItem:null;return(comp instanceof CompItem)?comp:null};
    $.global._aeHubGetLayer=function(cmd){var comp=$.global._aeHubGetActiveOrComp(cmd.compIndex);var lId = cmd.layerIndex || cmd.index || cmd.idx; if(!comp||!lId)return null;return comp.layer(lId)};
    $.global._aeHubGLT=function(layer){if(layer instanceof CameraLayer)return"camera";if(layer instanceof LightLayer)return"light";if(layer instanceof TextLayer)return"text";if(layer instanceof ShapeLayer)return"shape";if(layer instanceof AVLayer){if(layer.nullLayer)return"null";if(layer.source instanceof CompItem)return"comp";return"av"}return"unknown"};
    $.global._aeHubSV=function(val){if(val===null||val===undefined)return null;if(val instanceof Array){var arr=[];for(var i=0;i<val.length;i++)arr.push(val[i]);return arr}return val};
    $.global._aeHubGPT=function(parent){var props=[];var num=0;try{num=parent.numProperties}catch(e){return props}for(var i=1;i<=num;i++){var prop=parent.property(i);var info={index:i,name:prop.name,matchName:prop.matchName,propertyType:prop.propertyType,isGroup:false};try{info.isGroup=(prop.propertyType===PropertyType.INDEXED_GROUP||prop.propertyType===PropertyType.NAMED_GROUP)}catch(e){}if(info.isGroup){info.properties=$.global._aeHubGPT(prop)}else{try{info.value=$.global._aeHubSV(prop.value)}catch(e){info.value=null;info.error=e.toString()}try{info.isTimeVarying=prop.isTimeVarying;info.numKeys=prop.isTimeVarying?prop.numKeys:0;info.canSetExpression=prop.canSetExpression;info.propertyValueType=prop.propertyValueType;}catch(e){}}props.push(info)}return props};
    $.global._aeHubGPI=function(prop){var info={name:prop.name,matchName:prop.matchName};try{info.value=$.global._aeHubSV(prop.value)}catch(e){info.value=null}try{info.isTimeVarying=prop.isTimeVarying}catch(e){}try{info.numKeys=prop.isTimeVarying?prop.numKeys:0}catch(e){}try{info.expression=prop.expression}catch(e){}try{info.expressionEnabled=prop.expressionEnabled}catch(e){}return info};
    $.global._aeHubGBP=function(layer,pathStr){if(!pathStr)return null;var parts=pathStr.split("/");var current=layer;for(var i=0;i<parts.length;i++){if(!current||!current.property)return null;current=current.property(parts[i])}return current};
    $.global._aeHubGCE=function(){return[{name:"Gaussian Blur",matchName:"ADBE Gaussian Blur 2"},{name:"Brightness & Contrast",matchName:"ADBE Brightness & Contrast 2"},{name:"Hue/Saturation",matchName:"ADBE HUE SATURATION"},{name:"Levels",matchName:"ADBE Levels2"},{name:"Curves",matchName:"ADBE CurvesCustom"},{name:"Color Balance",matchName:"ADBE Color Balance"},{name:"Tint",matchName:"ADBE Tint"},{name:"Fill",matchName:"ADBE Fill"},{name:"Ramp",matchName:"ADBE Ramp"},{name:"Drop Shadow",matchName:"ADBE Drop Shadow"},{name:"Glow",matchName:"ADBE Glow 2"},{name:"Lightning",matchName:"ADBE Lightning 2"},{name:"Lens Flare",matchName:"ADBE Lens Flare"},{name:"Fractal Noise",matchName:"ADBE Turbulent Noise"},{name:"Shatter",matchName:"ADBE Shatter"},{name:"Wave Warp",matchName:"ADBE Wave Warp"},{name:"Spherize",matchName:"ADBE Spherize"},{name:"Twirl",matchName:"ADBE Twirl"},{name:"Displacement Map",matchName:"ADBE Displacement Map"},{name:"Corner Pin",matchName:"ADBE Corner Pin"},{name:"Motion Tile",matchName:"ADBE Motion Tile"},{name:"Echo",matchName:"ADBE Echo"},{name:"Posterize Time",matchName:"ADBE Posterize Time"},{name:"Sharpen",matchName:"ADBE Sharpen"},{name:"Unsharp mask",matchName:"ADBE Unsharp Mask"},{name:"Minimax",matchName:"ADBE Minimax"},{name:"Find Edges",matchName:"ADBE Find Edges"},{name:"Cartoon",matchName:"ADBE Cartoon"},{name:"Noise",matchName:"ADBE Noise"},{name:"Mosaic",matchName:"ADBE Mosaic"},{name:"Transform",matchName:"ADBE Geometry2"},{name:"Camera Lens Blur",matchName:"ADBE Camera Lens Blur"},{name:"Lumetri Color",matchName:"ADBE Lumetri"},{name:"Keylight 1.2",matchName:"Keylight"},{name:"3D Camera Tracker",matchName:"ADBE 3D Camera Tracker"},{name:"Warp Stabilizer",matchName:"ADBE Mocha"}]};

    app.scheduleTask("_aeHubPoll()",100,false);
    app.scheduleTask("_aeHubSync()",1000,false);
}else{
    alert("AE Control Hub: Cannot connect.\nMake sure server is running.");
}
})();
