import React from "react";
import { Layers, Copy, Zap } from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { Layer } from "@/src/lib/types";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface BlendingPanelProps {
  layer: Layer | null;
}

const AE_BLEND_MODES = [
  "Normal", "Dissolve", "Dancing Dissolve", "Darken", "Multiply", "Color Burn", "Linear Burn", "Darker Color",
  "Lighten", "Screen", "Color Dodge", "Linear Dodge", "Lighter Color", "Overlay", "Soft Light",
  "Hard Light", "Linear Light", "Vivid Light", "Pin Light", "Hard Mix", "Difference", "Exclusion",
  "Subtract", "Divide", "Hue", "Saturation", "Color", "Luminosity"
];

export const BlendingPanel: React.FC<BlendingPanelProps> = ({ layer }) => {
  if (!layer) return (
    <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
      <Layers size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-10" />
      <p className="text-xs uppercase font-black tracking-widest">Select a layer for blending options</p>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="panel-container">
      <div className="h-10 border-b border-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light flex items-center px-4 gap-2">
        <Copy size={14} className="text-tt-accent" />
        <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Blending & Opacity</span>
      </div>
      
      <div className="scrollable-content p-4 space-y-6">
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <label className="text-[9px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted">Blending Mode</label>
          <div className="relative">
             <select 
               className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-2.5 text-xs text-white appearance-none cursor-pointer focus:border-tt-accent focus:outline-none"
               onChange={(e) => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setBlendMode", idx: layer.index, mode: e.target.value })}
               defaultValue="Normal"
             >
               {AE_BLEND_MODES.map((mode) => (
                 <option key={mode} value={mode}>{mode}</option>
               ))}
             </select>
             <div className="absolute inset-y-0 right-3 flex items-center pointer-events-none text-tt-text-muted">
                <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"/></svg>
             </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="p-4 bg-tt-accent/5 border border-tt-accent/20 rounded-xl flex items-center gap-4">
           <Zap size={20} className="text-tt-accent shrink-0" />
           <p className="text-[10px] text-tt-text-muted italic leading-relaxed">
             Select a mode to apply it instantly to the active layer in After Effects.
           </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/CompSettings.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { X, Save, RotateCcw, Monitor, Clock, PlayCircle, Palette } from "lucide-react";
import { motion } from "motion/react";
import { Composition } from "@/src/lib/types";

interface CompSettingsProps {
  comp: Composition | null;
  onClose: () => void;
  onApply: (data: any) => void;
}

export const CompSettings: React.FC<CompSettingsProps> = ({ comp, onClose, onApply }) => {
  const [width, setWidth] = useState(comp?.width || 1920);
  const [height, setHeight] = useState(comp?.height || 1080);
  const [frameRate, setFrameRate] = useState(comp?.frameRate || 30);
  const [duration, setDuration] = useState(comp?.duration || 10);
  // Default AE background is black
  const [color, setColor] = useState("#000000"); 

  const handleApply = () => {
    // Convert hex to [r,g,b] 0-1 range
    const r = parseInt(color.slice(1, 3), 16) / 255;
    const g = parseInt(color.slice(3, 5), 16) / 255;
    const b = parseInt(color.slice(5, 7), 16) / 255;

    onApply({
      width: Number(width),
      height: Number(height),
      frameRate: Number(frameRate),
      duration: Number(duration),
      bgColor: [r, g, b]
    });
    onClose();
  };

  const handleReset = () => {
    if (comp) {
      setWidth(comp.width || 1920);
      setHeight(comp.height || 1080);
      setFrameRate(comp.frameRate || 30);
      setDuration(comp.duration || 10);
      setColor("#000000");
    }
  };

  const applyPreset = (w: number, h: number) => {
    setWidth(w);
    setHeight(h);
  };

  const applyMultiplier = (mult: number) => {
    setWidth(Math.round(width * mult));
    setHeight(Math.round(height * mult));
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 bg-black/80 backdrop-blur-md">
    <motion.div 
      initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
      className="w-full max-w-md bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-2xl shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden max-h-[90vh]"
    >
      <div className="h-14 border-b border-tt-border px-4 flex items-center justify-between bg-tt-surface-light shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <Monitor size={18} className="text-tt-accent" />
          <span className="text-sm font-black uppercase tracking-widest">{comp?.name || "Composition"} Settings</span>
        </div>
        <button onClick={onClose} className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5"><X size={18} /></button>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-6 custom-scrollbar">
        {/* Preset aspect ratios */}
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <h4 className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted uppercase tracking-tighter">Presets & Multipliers</h4>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1920, 1080)} className="px-2 py-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors">1080p (16:9)</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1080, 1920)} className="px-2 py-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors">Vertical (9:16)</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1080, 1080)} className="px-2 py-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors">Square (1:1)</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1080, 1350)} className="px-2 py-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors">Social (4:5)</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1440, 1080)} className="px-2 py-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors">SD (4:3)</button>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex gap-2 mt-2">
            <button onClick={() => applyMultiplier(0.5)} className="px-3 py-1 flex-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors font-bold">0.5x</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyMultiplier(2)} className="px-3 py-1 flex-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors font-bold">2x</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyMultiplier(3)} className="px-3 py-1 flex-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors font-bold">3x</button>
            <button onClick={() => applyMultiplier(4)} className="px-3 py-1 flex-1 text-[10px] bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded hover:border-tt-accent transition-colors font-bold">4x</button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Dimensions */}
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <h4 className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted uppercase tracking-tighter">Dimensions</h4>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <label htmlFor="comp-width" className="text-[9px] text-tt-text-muted ml-1">Width (px)</label>
              <input 
                id="comp-width" 
                name="comp-width" 
                type="number" 
                value={width} 
                onChange={(e) => setWidth(Number(e.target.value))}
                className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-3 text-sm font-mono focus:border-tt-accent outline-none" 
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <label htmlFor="comp-height" className="text-[9px] text-tt-text-muted ml-1">Height (px)</label>
              <input 
                id="comp-height" 
                name="comp-height" 
                type="number" 
                value={height} 
                onChange={(e) => setHeight(Number(e.target.value))}
                className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-3 text-sm font-mono focus:border-tt-accent outline-none" 
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Time Settings */}
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <h4 className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted uppercase tracking-tighter">Timeline & Appearance</h4>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <label htmlFor="comp-fps" className="text-[9px] text-tt-text-muted ml-1 flex items-center gap-1"><Clock size={8} /> Frame Rate</label>
              <select 
                id="comp-fps" 
                name="comp-fps" 
                value={frameRate} 
                onChange={(e) => setFrameRate(Number(e.target.value))}
                className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-3 text-sm focus:border-tt-accent outline-none appearance-none"
              >
                <option value="23.976" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">23.976</option>
                <option value="24" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">24</option>
                <option value="25" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">25</option>
                <option value="29.97" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">29.97</option>
                <option value="30" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">30</option>
                <option value="59.94" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">59.94</option>
                <option value="60" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">60</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <label htmlFor="comp-duration" className="text-[9px] text-tt-text-muted ml-1 flex items-center gap-1"><PlayCircle size={8} /> Duration (sec)</label>
              <input 
                id="comp-duration" 
                name="comp-duration" 
                type="number" 
                step="0.1"
                min="0.1"
                value={duration} 
                onChange={(e) => setDuration(Number(e.target.value))}
                className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-3 text-sm focus:border-tt-accent outline-none font-mono"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="space-y-3 mt-4">
            <label className="text-[9px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted uppercase tracking-tighter flex items-center gap-1"><Palette size={10} /> Background Color Preset</label>
            <div className="flex gap-2 mb-2">
               <button onClick={() => setColor("#000000")} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border border-tt-border hover:scale-110 transition-transform" style={{ backgroundColor: "#000000" }} title="Black (Default/Transparent)"></button>
               <button onClick={() => setColor("#ffffff")} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border border-tt-border hover:scale-110 transition-transform" style={{ backgroundColor: "#ffffff" }} title="White"></button>
               <button onClick={() => setColor("#555555")} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border border-tt-border hover:scale-110 transition-transform" style={{ backgroundColor: "#555555" }} title="Gray"></button>
               <button onClick={() => setColor("#00ff00")} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border border-tt-border hover:scale-110 transition-transform" style={{ backgroundColor: "#00ff00" }} title="Green Screen"></button>
               <button onClick={() => setColor("#0000ff")} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full border border-tt-border hover:scale-110 transition-transform" style={{ backgroundColor: "#0000ff" }} title="Blue Screen"></button>
            </div>
            <div className="flex bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-1.5 focus-within:border-tt-accent">
               <input 
                 type="color" 
                 value={color}
                 onChange={(e) => setColor(e.target.value)}
                 className="w-8 h-8 rounded shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-transparent border-0 p-0"
               />
               <div className="flex-1 px-3 flex flex-col justify-center">
                 <span className="text-xs font-mono text-tt-text-muted">{color.toUpperCase()}</span>
               </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="h-16 border-t border-tt-border px-4 flex items-center gap-3 bg-tt-surface-light shrink-0">
        <button onClick={handleReset} className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-white/5 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-colors">
          <RotateCcw size={14} /> Reset
        </button>
        <button 
          onClick={handleApply}
          className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-accent rounded-lg text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-white flex items-center justify-center gap-2 shadow-lg shadow-tt-accent/20 hover:bg-tt-accent-hover transition-colors"
        >
          <Save size={14} /> Apply Changes
        </button>
      </div>
    </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
};



------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/EffectsPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import {
  Search,
  Sparkles,
  Filter,
  Droplet,
  Sun,
  Wind,
  Box,
  Maximize,
  Scissors,
  Palette,
} from "lucide-react";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface EffectsPanelProps {
  selectedLayer: any;
}

export const EffectsPanel: React.FC<EffectsPanelProps> = ({
  selectedLayer,
}) => {
  const [effects, setEffects] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [category, setCategory] = useState<string>("All");

  useEffect(() => {
    socket
      .request("ae_command", { command: "getEffectsList" })
      .then((res: any) => {
        if (res && res.effects) {
          setEffects(res.effects);
        }
      });
  }, []);

  if (!selectedLayer) {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex items-center justify-center text-tt-text-muted bg-tt-bg">
        <p className="text-xs uppercase font-black tracking-widest">
          No layer selected
        </p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const getCategory = (name: string) => {
    const l = name.toLowerCase();
    if (
      l.includes("blur") ||
      l.includes("sharpen") ||
      l.includes("unsharp") ||
      l.includes("mosaic")
    )
      return "Blur / Sharpen";
    if (
      l.includes("color") ||
      l.includes("tint") ||
      l.includes("hue") ||
      l.includes("levels") ||
      l.includes("curves") ||
      l.includes("lumetri") ||
      l.includes("brightness")
    )
      return "Color & Light";
    if (
      l.includes("warp") ||
      l.includes("twirl") ||
      l.includes("spherize") ||
      l.includes("displacement") ||
      l.includes("tile") ||
      l.includes("transform") ||
      l.includes("shatter") ||
      l.includes("corner")
    )
      return "Distortion / Warp";
    if (
      l.includes("noise") ||
      l.includes("fractal") ||
      l.includes("lightning") ||
      l.includes("lens flare") ||
      l.includes("ramp") ||
      l.includes("fill") ||
      l.includes("drop shadow") ||
      l.includes("glow")
    )
      return "Generate / Decorate";
    if (
      l.includes("key") ||
      l.includes("cartoon") ||
      l.includes("find edges") ||
      l.includes("minimax") ||
      l.includes("echo") ||
      l.includes("posterize")
    )
      return "Stylize / Edge";
    return "Other";
  };

  const getIcon = (cat: string) => {
    if (cat === "Blur / Sharpen")
      return <Droplet size={14} className="text-blue-400" />;
    if (cat === "Color & Light")
      return <Sun size={14} className="text-yellow-400" />;
    if (cat === "Distortion / Warp")
      return <Wind size={14} className="text-orange-400" />;
    if (cat === "Generate / Decorate")
      return <Sparkles size={14} className="text-purple-400" />;
    if (cat === "Stylize / Edge")
      return <Palette size={14} className="text-pink-400" />;
    return <Box size={14} className="text-gray-400" />;
  };

  const filtered = effects.filter((e) => {
    if (search && !e.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()))
      return false;
    if (category !== "All" && getCategory(e.name) !== category) return false;
    return true;
  });

  const categories = [
    "All",
    "Color & Light",
    "Blur / Sharpen",
    "Distortion / Warp",
    "Generate / Decorate",
    "Stylize / Edge",
    "Other",
  ];

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col p-4 space-y-4 bg-tt-bg">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 h-10 bg-black/20 border border-tt-border rounded-xl px-3 shrink-0 focus-within:border-tt-accent transition-colors">
        <Search size={16} className="text-tt-text-muted" />
        <input
          type="text"
          value={search}
          onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Search Built-in Effects..."
          className="bg-transparent border-none outline-none text-xs w-full placeholder-tt-text-muted/50 text-tt-text"
        />
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 overflow-x-auto custom-scrollbar pb-2 shrink-0">
        {categories.map((cat) => (
          <button
            key={cat}
            onClick={() => setCategory(cat)}
            className={`whitespace-nowrap px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full border text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider transition-all flex items-center gap-1.5 ${category === cat ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent" : "bg-tt-surface-light border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white"}`}
          >
            {cat !== "All" && getIcon(cat)}
            {cat}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto pr-2 custom-scrollbar grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 content-start">
        {filtered.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center text-xs text-tt-text-muted mt-8 col-span-2">
            No effects found.
          </div>
        )}
        {filtered.map((effect) => {
          const cat = getCategory(effect.name);
          return (
            <button
              key={effect.matchName}
              onClick={() => {
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "addEffect",
                  layerIndex: selectedLayer.index,
                  effectMatchName: effect.matchName,
                });
              }}
              className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-4 bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded-xl hover:border-tt-accent hover:bg-tt-accent/10 transition-all text-left gap-3 group active:scale-95"
            >
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-black/40 flex items-center justify-center shadow-inner group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform">
                {getIcon(cat)}
              </div>
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text leading-tight text-center w-full truncate">
                {effect.name}
              </span>
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/GenericPropertiesPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { ScrubDial } from "./ScrubDial";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";
import { ChevronDown, ChevronRight, Layers } from "lucide-react";
import { throttle } from "@/src/lib/utils";

const AE_BLEND_MODES = [
  "Normal", "Dissolve", "Dancing Dissolve", "Darken", "Multiply", "Color Burn", "Linear Burn", "Darker Color",
  "Lighten", "Screen", "Color Dodge", "Linear Dodge", "Lighter Color", "Overlay", "Soft Light",
  "Hard Light", "Linear Light", "Vivid Light", "Pin Light", "Hard Mix", "Difference", "Exclusion",
  "Subtract", "Divide", "Hue", "Saturation", "Color", "Luminosity"
];

const PropertyValueType = {
  NO_VALUE: 5112,
  ThreeD_SPATIAL: 5113,
  ThreeD: 5114,
  TwoD_SPATIAL: 5115,
  TwoD: 5116,
  OneD: 5117,
  COLOR: 5118,
  CUSTOM_VALUE: 5119,
};

const throttledEmit = throttle(
  (event: string, data: any) => socket.emit(event, data),
  32,
);

const sendValue = (
  layerIdx: number,
  path: string[],
  val: any,
  isCommit: boolean = false,
) => {
  const pathStr = path
    .map((p) => `property('${p.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')`)
    .join(".");
  let valStr = Array.isArray(val) ? `[${val.join(",")}]` : val;
  const script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c&&c.layer(${layerIdx})){var p=c.layer(${layerIdx}).${pathStr}; if(p){if(p.numKeys>0){p.setValueAtTime(c.time, ${valStr});}else{p.setValue(${valStr});}}}`;

  if (isCommit) {
    socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "executeScript", script });
  } else {
    throttledEmit("ae_command", { command: "executeScript", script });
  }
};

const toggleKeyframe = (layerIdx: number, path: string[], hasKey: boolean) => {
  const pathStr = path
    .map((p) => `property('${p.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')`)
    .join(".");
  const script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c&&c.layer(${layerIdx})){var p=c.layer(${layerIdx}).${pathStr}; if(p && p.canSetExpression){ if(${hasKey}) { var ki = p.nearestKeyIndex(c.time); if(ki > 0 && Math.abs(p.keyTime(ki) - c.time) < 0.05) { p.removeKey(ki); } else { while(p.numKeys>0) p.removeKey(1); } } else { p.addKey(c.time); } }}`;
  socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "executeScript", script });
};

const PropertyGroup = ({ prop, layerIdx, path, filterType }: any) => {
  const isRelevant = React.useMemo(() => {
    if (!filterType) return true;
    const nameLower = prop.name.toLowerCase();
    const matchLower = prop.matchName.toLowerCase();
    if (filterType === "fill") {
      return (
        nameLower.includes("fill") ||
        nameLower.includes("color") ||
        matchLower.includes("fill") ||
        matchLower.includes("color") ||
        matchLower.includes("adbe root vectors group") ||
        matchLower.includes("adbe effect parade") ||
        matchLower.includes("adbe text properties")
      );
    }
    if (filterType === "border") {
      return (
        nameLower.includes("stroke") ||
        nameLower.includes("shadow") ||
        nameLower.includes("border") ||
        matchLower.includes("stroke") ||
        matchLower.includes("drop shadow") ||
        matchLower.includes("adbe root vectors group") ||
        matchLower.includes("adbe effect parade")
      );
    }
    return true;
  }, [prop.name, prop.matchName, filterType]);

  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(path.length <= 2);

  // Auto-expand if we're filtering and this group is considered relevant
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (filterType && isRelevant) setExpanded(true);
  }, [filterType, isRelevant]);

  const currentPath = [...path, prop.matchName];

  // If we are filtering, we skip rendering entirely if it's completely irrelevant
  // BUT we don't skip root groups like Effects/Contents if they contain relevant children
  // (the isRelevant check roughly covers this because we included vectors group and effect parade)
  if (filterType && !isRelevant && !prop.isGroup) return null;

  // A helper button for keyframes
  const KeyframeBtn = () => {
    if (!prop.canSetExpression) return null;
    const hasKey = prop.numKeys > 0;
    return (
      <button
        onClick={(e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          toggleKeyframe(layerIdx, currentPath, hasKey);
        }}
        className={`w-6 h-6 flex-shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center transition-colors group/key`}
        title="Toggle Keyframe"
      >
        <div
          className={`w-3 h-3 rotate-45 border-2 transition-all ${
             hasKey ? "border-tt-warning bg-tt-warning shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(255,214,0,0.6)]" : "border-tt-text-muted bg-transparent group-hover/key:border-tt-text group-hover/key:bg-tt-text-muted/20"
          }`}
        />
      </button>
    );
  };

  if (prop.isGroup) {
    // Only show groups if they have renderable properties
    if (!prop.properties || prop.properties.length === 0) return null;
    return (
      <div className="border border-tt-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden mb-2 bg-tt-surface/30">
        <button
          onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}
          className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 flex items-center justify-between hover:bg-white/5"
        >
          <div className="flex gap-2 items-center text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted">
            <Layers size={10} /> {prop.name}
          </div>
          {expanded ? <ChevronDown size={12} /> : <ChevronRight size={12} />}
        </button>
        {expanded && (
          <div className="p-2 border-t border-tt-border flex flex-col gap-2">
            {prop.properties.map((child: any) => (
              <PropertyGroup
                key={child.matchName + child.name}
                prop={child}
                layerIdx={layerIdx}
                path={currentPath}
                filterType={filterType}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Not a group, render input based on type
  if (prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.OneD) {
    return (
      <div className="flex gap-2 items-center">
        <KeyframeBtn />
        <div className="flex-1">
          <ScrubDial
            label={prop.name}
            value={prop.value || 0}
            onChange={(v) => sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, v)}
            onCommit={(v) => sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, v, true)}
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  } else if (
    prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.TwoD ||
    prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.TwoD_SPATIAL
  ) {
    return (
      <div className="flex gap-2 items-center">
        <KeyframeBtn />
        <div className="flex-1 flex bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden group">
          <div className="px-2 py-1.5 bg-black/20 w-24 flex flex-shrink-0 items-center text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted">
            {prop.name}
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 grid grid-cols-2 divide-x divide-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light">
            <ScrubDial
              label="X"
              value={prop.value?.[0] || 0}
              onChange={(v) =>
                sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, [v, prop.value?.[1] || 0])
              }
              onCommit={(v) =>
                sendValue(
                  layerIdx,
                  currentPath,
                  [v, prop.value?.[1] || 0],
                  true,
                )
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Y"
              value={prop.value?.[1] || 0}
              onChange={(v) =>
                sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, [prop.value?.[0] || 0, v])
              }
              onCommit={(v) =>
                sendValue(
                  layerIdx,
                  currentPath,
                  [prop.value?.[0] || 0, v],
                  true,
                )
              }
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  } else if (
    prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.ThreeD ||
    prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.ThreeD_SPATIAL
  ) {
    return (
      <div className="flex gap-2 items-center">
        <KeyframeBtn />
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden group">
          <div className="px-2 py-1.5 bg-black/20 flex flex-shrink-0 items-center text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted">
            {prop.name}
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 divide-x divide-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light">
            <ScrubDial
              label="X"
              value={prop.value?.[0] || 0}
              onChange={(v) =>
                sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, [
                  v,
                  prop.value?.[1] || 0,
                  prop.value?.[2] || 0,
                ])
              }
              onCommit={(v) =>
                sendValue(
                  layerIdx,
                  currentPath,
                  [v, prop.value?.[1] || 0, prop.value?.[2] || 0],
                  true,
                )
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Y"
              value={prop.value?.[1] || 0}
              onChange={(v) =>
                sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, [
                  prop.value?.[0] || 0,
                  v,
                  prop.value?.[2] || 0,
                ])
              }
              onCommit={(v) =>
                sendValue(
                  layerIdx,
                  currentPath,
                  [prop.value?.[0] || 0, v, prop.value?.[2] || 0],
                  true,
                )
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Z"
              value={prop.value?.[2] || 0}
              onChange={(v) =>
                sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, [
                  prop.value?.[0] || 0,
                  prop.value?.[1] || 0,
                  v,
                ])
              }
              onCommit={(v) =>
                sendValue(
                  layerIdx,
                  currentPath,
                  [prop.value?.[0] || 0, prop.value?.[1] || 0, v],
                  true,
                )
              }
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  } else if (prop.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.COLOR) {
    // AE uses 0-1 for RGB
    const toHex = (c: number[]) => {
      if (!c) return "#000000";
      return (
        "#" +
        c
          .slice(0, 3)
          .map((x) =>
            Math.round(Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x)) * 255)
              .toString(16)
              .padStart(2, "0"),
          )
          .join("")
      );
    };
    const fromHex = (h: string) => {
      return [
        parseInt(h.substring(1, 3), 16) / 255,
        parseInt(h.substring(3, 5), 16) / 255,
        parseInt(h.substring(5, 7), 16) / 255,
        1,
      ];
    };
    return (
      <div className="flex gap-2 items-center">
        <KeyframeBtn />
        <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-between p-2 bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-lg group">
          <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted group-hover:text-tt-text transition-colors">
            {prop.name}
          </span>
          <input
            type="color"
            value={toHex(prop.value)}
            onChange={(e) =>
              sendValue(layerIdx, currentPath, fromHex(e.target.value))
            }
            className="w-12 h-6 rounded cursor-pointer p-0 border-0 bg-transparent"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return null;
};

export const GenericPropertiesPanel = ({
  layer,
  filterType,
}: {
  layer: any;
  filterType?: string;
}) => {
  if (!layer || !layer.rawProperties) return null;
  // Filter out the transform group as we already have a specialized panel for it
  let props = layer.rawProperties;

  // Optional domain specific filtering based on filterType
  let title = "All Properties";

  if (filterType === "fill") {
    title = "Color & Fill";
    // For shape layers, we want Contents
    // For text layers, maybe Animators or Effects
    // Usually, Fill effect is under Effects
  } else if (filterType === "border") {
    title = "Border & Shadow";
  } else if (filterType === "shapes") {
    title = "Shape Controls";
    props = props.filter((p: any) => p.matchName === "ADBE Root Vectors Group");
  } else if (filterType === "text") {
    title = "Text Controls";
    props = props.filter((p: any) => p.matchName === "ADBE Text Properties");
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
      {/* Layer Base Settings (Blend Mode) - Only show if not filtering specifically */}
      {!filterType && (
         <div className="border border-tt-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden bg-tt-surface/30">
            <div className="px-3 py-2 border-b border-tt-border/50 bg-black/10 flex items-center justify-between">
               <span className="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-accent">Base Layer Properties</span>
            </div>
            <div className="p-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
               <div>
                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted tracking-widest block mb-1">Blending Mode</label>
                 <div className="relative">
                   <select 
                     className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border hover:border-tt-text-muted rounded-lg p-1.5 pl-2 pr-6 text-xs text-tt-text appearance-none cursor-pointer transition-colors"
                     value={layer.blendMode || "Normal"}
                     onChange={(e) => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setBlendMode", idx: layer.index, mode: e.target.value })}
                   >
                     {AE_BLEND_MODES.map((mode) => (
                       <option key={mode} value={mode}>{mode}</option>
                     ))}
                   </select>
                   <ChevronDown size={12} className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-tt-text-muted pointer-events-none" />
                 </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted tracking-widest block mb-1">Time Stretch</label>
                 <div className="relative flex items-center group">
                    <input 
                      type="number"
                      className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border group-hover:border-tt-text-muted rounded-lg p-1.5 pl-2 pr-6 text-xs text-tt-text transition-colors text-right font-mono"
                      value={layer.timeStretch || 100}
                      onChange={(e) => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setTimeStretch", layerIndex: layer.index, stretchResult: parseFloat(e.target.value) })}
                    />
                    <span className="absolute right-2 text-xs text-tt-text-muted pointer-events-none">%</span>
                 </div>
               </div>
            </div>
         </div>
      )}

      {props.length > 0 && (
         <div className="flex flex-col">
           <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
             <h3 className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-tt-accent">
               {title}
             </h3>
             <div className="h-px bg-tt-border flex-1" />
           </div>
           <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
             {props.map((p: any) => (
               <PropertyGroup
                 key={p.matchName}
                 prop={p}
                 layerIdx={layer.index}
                 path={[]}
                 filterType={filterType}
               />
             ))}
           </div>
         </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

            <span className="font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm">Touch Tools Guide</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-2 space-y-1 flex md:flex-col overflow-x-auto md:overflow-x-hidden snap-x">
            {topics.map(topic => (
              <button
                key={topic.id}
                onClick={() => setActiveTopic(topic.id)}
                className={`flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-3 rounded-xl transition-all text-left whitespace-nowrap md:whitespace-normal snap-start ${
                  activeTopic === topic.id 
                    ? 'bg-tt-accent text-white shadow-lg shadow-tt-accent/20' 
                    : 'text-tt-text-muted hover:bg-white/5 hover:text-tt-text'
                }`}
              >
                <div className={activeTopic === topic.id ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-70'}>
                  {topic.icon}
                </div>
                <span className="font-bold text-xs uppercase tracking-wider">{topic.title}</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col bg-tt-bg relative">
          <button 
            onClick={onClose}
            className="absolute top-4 right-4 tt-button-icon !p-2 bg-tt-surface shadow-lg z-10"
          >
            <X size={16} />
          </button>
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 md:p-8">
            <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
              <motion.div
                key={activeTopic}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
              >
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-black mb-6 text-tt-text flex items-center gap-3">
                  {topics.find(t => t.id === activeTopic)?.icon}
                  {topics.find(t => t.id === activeTopic)?.title}
                </h2>
                {topics.find(t => t.id === activeTopic)?.content}
              </motion.div>
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/KeyframesPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import {
  Key,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  Trash2,
  Plus,
  Clock,
  Activity,
  Copy,
  ClipboardPaste,
} from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { Layer } from "@/src/lib/types";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface KeyframesPanelProps {
  layer: Layer | null;
}

export const KeyframesPanel: React.FC<KeyframesPanelProps> = ({ layer }) => {
  const [activeEase, setActiveEase] = useState("linear");

  if (!layer) {
    return (
      <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
        <Key size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-10" />
        <p className="text-xs uppercase font-black tracking-widest">
          Select a layer for keyframe work
        </p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const getKeyedProps = () => {
    const keyed = [];
    const t = layer.properties.transform;
    if (t.position.hasKeyframes)
      keyed.push({ name: "Position", val: t.position.value });
    if (t.scale.hasKeyframes)
      keyed.push({ name: "Scale", val: t.scale.value[0] });
    if (t.rotation.hasKeyframes)
      keyed.push({ name: "Rotation", val: t.rotation.value });
    if (t.opacity.hasKeyframes)
      keyed.push({ name: "Opacity", val: t.opacity.value });
    return keyed;
  };

  const keyedProps = getKeyedProps();

  const handleApplyEase = (type: string) => {
    setActiveEase(type);
    let influence = 33.3;
    let speed = 0;
    if (type === "easeIn") {
      influence = 50;
    } else if (type === "easeOut") {
      influence = 50;
    } else if (type === "easeInOut") {
      influence = 75;
    }

    socket.emit("ae_command", {
      command: "executeScript",
      script: `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${layer.index});
      var props = [l.property('Transform').property('Position'), l.property('Transform').property('Scale'), l.property('Transform').property('Rotation'), l.property('Transform').property('Opacity')];
      var easeIn = new KeyframeEase(0, ${influence});
      var easeOut = new KeyframeEase(0, ${influence});
      for(var i=0; i<props.length; i++) {
        var p = props[i];
        if (p && p.numKeys > 0) {
          try {
             for(var k=1; k<=p.numKeys; k++) {
                if(p.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.TwoD_SPATIAL || p.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.ThreeD_SPATIAL || p.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.ThreeD) {
                   p.setTemporalEaseAtKey(k, [easeIn, easeIn, easeIn], [easeOut, easeOut, easeOut]);
                } else if(p.propertyValueType === PropertyValueType.TwoD) {
                   p.setTemporalEaseAtKey(k, [easeIn, easeIn], [easeOut, easeOut]);
                } else {
                   p.setTemporalEaseAtKey(k, [easeIn], [easeOut]);
                }
             }
          } catch(e){}
        }
      }
      }`,
    });
  };

  return (
    <div className="panel-container flex-1">
      <div className="h-10 border-b border-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light flex items-center px-4 justify-between shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Key size={14} className="text-tt-accent" />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">
            Keyframe Console
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="scrollable-content p-4 space-y-4">
        <div className="bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-xl p-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text">
              <Activity size={12} className="text-tt-warning" />
              Graph Editor / Easing
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <button
                className="p-1.5 hover:bg-white/10 rounded border border-tt-border hover:border-white/20 text-tt-text-muted transition-colors"
                title="Copy Curve"
              >
                <Copy size={12} />
              </button>
              <button
                className="p-1.5 hover:bg-white/10 rounded border border-tt-border hover:border-white/20 text-tt-text-muted transition-colors"
                title="Paste Curve"
              >
                <ClipboardPaste size={12} />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="aspect-[2/1] w-full bg-black/40 rounded border border-white/5 relative overflow-hidden mb-4">
            {/* Graph visualization placeholder mimicking ALight Motion */}
            <svg
              viewBox="0 0 100 50"
              className="w-full h-full text-tt-accent stroke-current opacity-70"
            >
              <path
                d={
                  activeEase === "linear"
                    ? "M 10 40 L 90 10"
                    : activeEase === "easeIn"
                      ? "M 10 40 C 50 40, 70 10, 90 10"
                      : activeEase === "easeOut"
                        ? "M 10 40 C 30 40, 50 10, 90 10"
                        : "M 10 40 C 40 40, 60 10, 90 10"
                }
                fill="none"
                strokeWidth="2"
                strokeLinecap="round"
              />
              <circle cx="10" cy="40" r="3" fill="currentColor" />
              <circle cx="90" cy="10" r="3" fill="currentColor" />
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-[0.05] bg-[linear-gradient(rgba(255,255,255,1)_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,1)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:10%_10%]" />
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2">
            <button
              onClick={() => handleApplyEase("linear")}
              className={cn(
                "py-2 rounded-lg border text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all tracking-wider text-center",
                activeEase === "linear"
                  ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent"
                  : "bg-tt-surface-light border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
              )}
            >
              Linear
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => handleApplyEase("easeIn")}
              className={cn(
                "py-2 rounded-lg border text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all tracking-wider text-center",
                activeEase === "easeIn"
                  ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent"
                  : "bg-tt-surface-light border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
              )}
            >
              Ease In
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => handleApplyEase("easeOut")}
              className={cn(
                "py-2 rounded-lg border text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all tracking-wider text-center",
                activeEase === "easeOut"
                  ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent"
                  : "bg-tt-surface-light border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
              )}
            >
              Ease Out
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => handleApplyEase("easeInOut")}
              className={cn(
                "py-2 rounded-lg border text-[9px] font-bold uppercase transition-all tracking-wider text-center",
                activeEase === "easeInOut"
                  ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent"
                  : "bg-tt-surface-light border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
              )}
            >
              In-Out
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-4 mb-2">
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-tt-text-muted">
            Active Properties
          </span>
          <div className="h-px bg-tt-border flex-1" />
        </div>

        {keyedProps.length > 0 ? (
          keyedProps.map((prop, i) => (
            <div
              key={i}
              className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-xl"
            >
              <div className="flex flex-col">
                <span className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted">
                  Property
                </span>
                <span className="text-xs font-black">{prop.name}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex flex-col items-end">
                <span className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted">
                  Current
                </span>
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono font-bold">
                  {typeof prop.val === "object"
                    ? prop.val.join(", ")
                    : prop.val}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        ) : (
          <div className="py-12 text-center opacity-30 italic text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest">
            No active keyframes found
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/LayerActionSheet.tsx

import React from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "motion/react";
import {
  X,
  Move,
  Droplet,
  Palette,
  Wand2,
  Scissors,
  SquareDashedBottom,
  Clock,
  LayoutTemplate,
  Zap,
} from "lucide-react";
import { Layer } from "../lib/types";
import { cn } from "../lib/utils";

export const LayerActionSheet = ({
  layer,
  isOpen,
  onClose,
  onOpenTab,
}: {
  layer: Layer | null;
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  onOpenTab: (tab: string) => void;
}) => {
  if (!layer) return null;

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {isOpen && (
        <>
          {/* Backdrop */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-md z-40"
            onClick={onClose}
          />
          {/* Bottom Sheet */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ y: "100%" }}
            animate={{ y: 0 }}
            exit={{ y: "100%" }}
            transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
            className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 h-[65vh] bg-tt-bg border-t border-tt-border z-50 rounded-t-[2rem] shadow-[0_-20px_50px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5)] flex flex-col overflow-hidden"
          >
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-5 border-b border-white/5">
              <div className="flex flex-col">
                <span className="text-sm font-black text-tt-text truncate">
                  {layer.name}
                </span>
                <span className="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase text-tt-accent tracking-widest">
                  {layer.layerType || layer.type} layer
                </span>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={onClose}
                className="p-2 bg-tt-surface-light hover:bg-white/10 rounded-full transition-colors border border-tt-border hover:border-white/20"
              >
                <X size={16} className="text-tt-text" />
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 bg-gradient-to-b from-tt-surface-light to-tt-bg custom-scrollbar">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Palette}
                  label="Color & Fill"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("properties")}
                  color="text-yellow-400"
                  bg="bg-yellow-400/5 hover:bg-yellow-400/10"
                  border="border-yellow-400/10 hover:border-yellow-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={SquareDashedBottom}
                  label="Border & Shadow"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("properties")}
                  color="text-orange-400"
                  bg="bg-orange-400/5 hover:bg-orange-400/10"
                  border="border-orange-400/10 hover:border-orange-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Droplet}
                  label="Blending & Opacity"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("blending")}
                  color="text-pink-400"
                  bg="bg-pink-400/5 hover:bg-pink-400/10"
                  border="border-pink-400/10 hover:border-pink-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Move}
                  label="Move & Transform"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("transform")}
                  color="text-blue-400"
                  bg="bg-blue-400/5 hover:bg-blue-400/10"
                  border="border-blue-400/10 hover:border-blue-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Wand2}
                  label="Effects"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("effects")}
                  color="text-green-400"
                  bg="bg-green-400/5 hover:bg-green-400/10"
                  border="border-green-400/10 hover:border-green-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={LayoutTemplate}
                  label="Edit Shape / Masks"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("masks")}
                  color="text-red-400"
                  bg="bg-red-400/5 hover:bg-red-400/10"
                  border="border-red-400/10 hover:border-red-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Clock}
                  label="Timer / Speed"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("speed")}
                  color="text-teal-400"
                  bg="bg-teal-400/5 hover:bg-teal-400/10"
                  border="border-teal-400/10 hover:border-teal-400/30"
                />
                <ActionCard
                  icon={Zap}
                  label="Keyframes"
                  onClick={() => onOpenTab("keyframes")}
                  color="text-tt-accent"
                  bg="bg-tt-accent/5 hover:bg-tt-accent/10"
                  border="border-tt-accent/10 hover:border-tt-accent/30"
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
};

const ActionCard = ({ icon: Icon, label, onClick, color, bg, border }: any) => {
  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 rounded-2xl transition-all group aspect-square border",
        bg,
        border,
      )}
    >
      <div
        className={cn(
          "p-4 rounded-full mb-4 bg-black/20 group-hover:bg-black/40 shadow-inner",
          color,
        )}
      >
        <Icon
          size={32}
          className="transition-transform group-hover:scale-110"
        />
      </div>
      <span className="text-[12px] font-black text-tt-text text-center leading-tight">
        {label}
      </span>
    </button>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/LayersPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { 
  Eye, 
  EyeOff, 
  Plus, 
  RotateCcw, 
  Layers as LayersIcon,
  Search,
  ChevronDown,
  Box,
  Type,
  Video,
  Sun,
  MousePointer2,
  File,
  Circle,
  Lock,
  Unlock,
  Ghost,
  Zap,
  Volume2,
  VolumeX,
  Copy,
  Trash2,
  Scissors,
  Folder,
  SquareDashedBottom
} from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { Layer, LayerType } from "@/src/lib/types";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface LayersPanelProps {
  layers: Layer[];
  selectedIndices: number[];
  onSelect: (index: number, multi: boolean) => void;
  onDoubleClick: (index: number) => void;
  onToggleVisibility: (index: number) => void;
  onToggleLock: (index: number) => void;
  onToggleSolo: (index: number) => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  onAddLayer: (type: string) => void;
  activeLayer: any;
  currentTime: number;
  duration: number;
  isPlaying: boolean;
  onTogglePlay: () => void;
  onSeek: (time: number) => void;
  onStep: (frames: number) => void;
}

import { GenericPropertiesPanel } from "./GenericPropertiesPanel";
import { TimelineBar } from "./TimelineBar";

const LayerIcon = ({ type }: { type: LayerType }) => {
  switch (type) {
    case "Shape": return <Box size={14} className="text-tt-warning" />;
    case "Text": return <Type size={14} className="text-tt-accent" />;
    case "Camera": return <Video size={14} className="text-tt-text-muted" />;
    case "Light": return <Sun size={14} className="text-tt-warning" />;
    case "Adjustment": return <Circle size={14} className="text-tt-accent fill-current" />;
    case "Null": return <MousePointer2 size={14} className="text-tt-text-muted opacity-50" />;
    default: return <File size={14} className="text-tt-text-muted" />;
  }
};

import { useLongPress } from "@/src/hooks/useLongPress";

const LayerRow = ({ layer, isSelected, onSelect, onDoubleClick, onToggleVisibility, onToggleSolo, onToggleLock }: any) => {
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);

  const bind = useLongPress(
    () => {
      console.log("Long press on layer", layer.index);
    },
    (e: any) => {
      onSelect(layer.index, e.shiftKey);
    }
  );

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col border-b border-tt-border/50 bg-tt-surface-light group/row">
      <div 
        {...bind}
        draggable
        onDragStart={(e) => { e.dataTransfer.setData("text/plain", layer.index.toString()); }}
        onDragOver={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
        onDrop={(e) => {
          e.preventDefault();
          const fromIndex = parseInt(e.dataTransfer.getData("text/plain"));
          const toIndex = layer.index;
          if (fromIndex && toIndex && fromIndex !== toIndex) {
            socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "reorderLayer", layerIndex: fromIndex, toIndex: toIndex });
          }
        }}
        onDoubleClick={(e) => {
           e.stopPropagation();
           onDoubleClick(layer.index);
           setIsExpanded(!isExpanded);
        }}
        onClick={(e) => {
           e.stopPropagation();
           onSelect(layer.index, e.shiftKey || e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey);
        }}
        className={cn(
          "group flex items-center h-10 px-2 gap-2 interactive-bg-pure transition-all cursor-pointer pl-1 pr-3 relative",
          isSelected && "bg-blue-500/15 border-l-4 border-blue-500 shadow-[inset_10px_0_20px_-10px_rgba(59,130,246,0.15)]"
        )}
      >
      <span className={cn(
        "text-[8px] font-mono w-4 flex-none text-center",
        isSelected ? "text-tt-accent font-bold" : "text-tt-text-muted opacity-40"
      )}>
        {layer.index.toString().padStart(2, '0')}
      </span>
      
      <button 
        onClick={(e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          onToggleVisibility(layer.index);
        }}
        onDoubleClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        className={cn(
          "flex-none w-8 h-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded transition-colors",
          layer.enabled ? "text-tt-text hover:text-tt-accent" : "text-tt-text-muted opacity-40 hover:opacity-100"
        )}
      >
        {layer.enabled ? <Eye size={14} /> : <EyeOff size={14} />}
      </button>

      <div 
        className="flex items-center gap-0.5 ml-1 mr-2 opacity-30 group-hover:opacity-100 focus-within:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
        onDoubleClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <button 
          onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onToggleSolo(layer.index); }}
          className={cn("w-5 h-5 flex items-center justify-center rounded text-[10px] font-bold border transition-colors", layer.solo ? "bg-cyan-500/20 text-cyan-400 border-cyan-500/50" : "bg-transparent border-transparent text-tt-text-muted hover:bg-white/5 hover:border-tt-border")}
          title="Solo Player"
        >
          <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full border border-current" />
        </button>
        <button 
          onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onToggleLock(layer.index); }}
          className={cn("w-5 h-5 flex items-center justify-center rounded text-tt-text-muted border transition-colors", layer.locked ? "bg-tt-warning/20 text-tt-warning border-tt-warning/50" : "bg-transparent border-transparent hover:bg-white/5 hover:border-tt-border")}
          title="Lock Layer"
        >
          {layer.locked ? <Lock size={10} /> : <Unlock size={10} className="opacity-40" />}
        </button>
      </div>

      <LayerIcon type={layer.type} />

      <span className={cn(
        "flex-1 text-xs truncate font-medium tracking-tight px-1",
        !layer.enabled && "text-tt-text-muted italic opacity-50"
      )}>
        {layer.name}
      </span>

      <div 
        className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-none translate-x-2 group-hover:translate-x-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all"
        onDoubleClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        {layer.hasAudio && (
          <button 
             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setLayerProperty", property: "audioEnabled", value: !layer.audioEnabled, layerIndex: layer.index }); }}
             className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text bg-tt-surface-light rounded-sm" title="Toggle audio"
          >
             {layer.audioEnabled ? <Volume2 size={12} /> : <VolumeX size={12} className="opacity-50" />}
          </button>
        )}
        <button 
           onClick={async (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); await socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "addMask", idx: layer.index, name: "New Mask" }); setTimeout(() => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "refresh" }), 100); }}
           className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-accent bg-tt-surface-light rounded-sm" title="Add Mask"
        >
           <SquareDashedBottom size={12} />
        </button>
        <button 
           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "splitLayer", layerIndex: layer.index }); }}
           className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white bg-tt-surface-light rounded-sm" title="Split layer at playhead"
        >
           <Scissors size={12} />
        </button>
        <button 
           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "duplicateLayer", layerIndex: layer.index }); }}
           className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white bg-tt-surface-light rounded-sm" title="Duplicate layer"
        >
           <Copy size={12} />
        </button>
        <button 
           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "deleteLayer", layerIndex: layer.index }); }}
           className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-error/60 hover:text-tt-error bg-tt-error/10 rounded-sm" title="Delete layer"
        >
           <Trash2 size={12} />
        </button>
        
        {layer.flags?.effects && <Zap size={10} className="text-tt-accent" />}
        <button 
           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onSelect(layer.index, false); setIsExpanded(!isExpanded); }}
           className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white ml-1"
        >
           <ChevronDown size={14} className={cn("transition-transform", isExpanded && "rotate-180")} />
        </button>
      </div>
      </div>
      
      {isExpanded && isSelected && (
        <div className="pl-6 pr-2 py-2 border-l-2 border-blue-500 bg-tt-bg">
           {layer.rawProperties ? (
              <GenericPropertiesPanel layer={layer} />
           ) : (
              <div className="text-[10px] text-tt-text-muted flex items-center justify-center p-4">Select to load properties...</div>
           )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export const LayersPanel: React.FC<LayersPanelProps> = ({
  layers,
  selectedIndices,
  onSelect,
  onDoubleClick,
  onToggleVisibility,
  onToggleLock,
  onToggleSolo,
  onRefresh,
  onAddLayer,
  activeLayer,
  currentTime,
  duration,
  isPlaying,
  onTogglePlay,
  onSeek,
  onStep
}) => {
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  
  const filteredLayers = layers.filter(l => 
    l.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || 
    l.index.toString() === search
  );

  return (
    <div className="panel-container">
      {/* Embedded Timeline Below Composition View, Pinned to Top of Layers Area (Light Motion Style) */}
      <TimelineBar 
        currentTime={currentTime}
        duration={duration}
        isPlaying={isPlaying}
        activeLayer={activeLayer}
        onTogglePlay={onTogglePlay}
        onSeek={onSeek}
        onStep={onStep}
      />

      {/* 15. Layer Toolbar */}
      <div className="h-10 border-b border-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light flex items-center px-2 gap-1 shrink-0">
        <button onClick={onRefresh} className="tt-button-icon" title="Refresh List">
          <RotateCcw size={16} />
        </button>
        <div className="h-4 w-px bg-tt-border mx-1" />
        <button onClick={() => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "groupLayers" })} className="tt-button-icon text-tt-accent" title="Group Selected (Pre-compose)">
          <Folder size={16} />
        </button>
        <button onClick={() => onAddLayer("shape")} className="tt-button-icon" title="Add Shape Layer">
          <Plus size={16} />
        </button>
        <div className="flex-1" />
        <div className="relative">
          <label htmlFor="layer-search" className="sr-only">Search Layers</label>
          <Search size={14} className="absolute left-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-tt-text-muted" />
          <input 
            id="layer-search"
            name="layer-search"
            type="text" 
            placeholder="Search layers..." 
            value={search}
            onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
            className="bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-md pl-8 pr-2 py-1 text-xs focus:outline-none focus:border-tt-accent w-32 focus:w-48 transition-all"
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 14. Layer List */}
      <div className="scrollable-content">
        {filteredLayers.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-tt-text-muted p-8 text-center animate-pulse">
            <LayersIcon size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-20" />
            <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest font-bold mb-2">{search ? "No matches found" : "No Layers Found"}</p>
            <p className="text-[10px] opacity-60">{search ? "Try a different query" : "Connect to AE or check current composition"}</p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="divide-y divide-tt-border/50">
            {filteredLayers.map((layer) => (
              <LayerRow 
                key={layer.index}
                layer={layer}
                isSelected={selectedIndices.includes(layer.index)}
                onSelect={onSelect}
                onDoubleClick={onDoubleClick}
                onToggleVisibility={onToggleVisibility}
                onToggleSolo={onToggleSolo}
                onToggleLock={onToggleLock}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/MasksPanel.tsx

import React from "react";
import { 
  PenTool, 
  Eye, 
  EyeOff, 
  Trash2, 
  Plus,
  Maximize2
} from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { Layer } from "@/src/lib/types";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface MasksPanelProps {
  layer: Layer | null;
}

export const MasksPanel: React.FC<MasksPanelProps> = ({ layer }) => {
  if (!layer) {
    return (
      <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
        <PenTool size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-10" />
        <p className="text-xs uppercase font-black tracking-widest">Select a layer to edit masks</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="panel-container">
      <div className="h-12 border-b border-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light flex items-center px-4 justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <PenTool size={14} className="text-tt-accent" />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Mask Management</span>
        </div>
        <button 
          onClick={async () => {
            await socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "addMask", idx: layer.index, name: "New Mask" });
            setTimeout(() => {
              socket.request("ae_command", { command: "getMasks", idx: layer.index }).then((res: any) => {
                if (res && res.masks) {
                   socket.triggerLocal("ui_state_update", {
                      layers: [{ index: layer.index, masks: res.masks }]
                   });
                }
              }).catch(() => {});
            }, 100);
          }}
          className="tt-button-icon bg-tt-accent/10 text-tt-accent"
        >
          <Plus size={16} />
        </button>
      </div>

      <div className="scrollable-content p-4 space-y-2">
        {layer.masks && layer.masks.length > 0 ? (
          layer.masks.map((mask, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-xl p-3 flex flex-col gap-3 group">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                 <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-tt-accent" />
                    <span className="text-xs font-bold font-mono">{mask.name}</span>
                 </div>
                 <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                    <button 
                      onClick={async () => {
                        await socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "toggleInvert", idx: layer.index, maskIndex: i + 1 });
                        setTimeout(() => {
                           socket.request("ae_command", { command: "getMasks", idx: layer.index }).then((res: any) => {
                             if (res && res.masks) {
                                socket.triggerLocal("ui_state_update", { layers: [{ index: layer.index, masks: res.masks }] });
                             }
                           }).catch(() => {});
                        }, 100);
                      }}
                      className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5 outline-none"
                    >
                      {mask.inverted ? <EyeOff size={14} className="text-tt-warning" /> : <Eye size={14} />}
                    </button>
                    <button 
                      onClick={async () => {
                        await socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "removeMask", idx: layer.index, maskIndex: i + 1 });
                        setTimeout(() => {
                           socket.request("ae_command", { command: "getMasks", idx: layer.index }).then((res: any) => {
                             if (res) { // res.masks might be undefined if 0 masks
                                socket.triggerLocal("ui_state_update", { layers: [{ index: layer.index, masks: res.masks || [] }] });
                             }
                           }).catch(() => {});
                        }, 100);
                      }}
                      className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5 hover:text-tt-error"
                    >
                      <Trash2 size={14} />
                    </button>
                 </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                 <div className="bg-tt-bg rounded px-2 py-1.5 flex flex-col relative group/mode">
                    <label htmlFor={`mask-mode-${mask.name}`} className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted">Mode</label>
                    <select 
                      id={`mask-mode-${mask.name}`}
                      name={`mask-mode-${mask.name}`}
                      className="text-[10px] font-bold bg-transparent border-none p-0 focus:ring-0 appearance-none cursor-pointer"
                      value={mask.mode}
                      onChange={(e) => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setMaskMode", idx: layer.index, maskIndex: i + 1, mode: parseInt(e.target.value) })}
                    >
                      {["None", "Add", "Subtract", "Intersect", "Lighten", "Darken", "Difference"].map((m, idx) => (
                        <option key={m} value={idx} className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">{m}</option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                 </div>
                 <div className="bg-tt-bg rounded px-2 py-1.5 flex flex-col">
                    <span className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold text-tt-text-muted">Status</span>
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold">{mask.inverted ? "Inverted" : "Normal"}</span>
                 </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        ) : (
          <div className="py-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted opacity-30 italic text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest">
            No masks applied to this layer
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

import React from "react";

  { id: "transform", label: "Transform", icon: MousePointer2 },
  { id: "effects", label: "Effects", icon: Zap },
  { id: "blending", label: "Blending", icon: Copy },
  { id: "shapes", label: "Shapes", icon: Box },
  { id: "text", label: "Text", icon: Type },
  { id: "keyframes", label: "Keys", icon: Key },

export const Navigation: React.FC<NavigationProps> = ({ activeTab, onTabChange, hasSelection }) => {

              )}

              <Icon size={16} strokeWidth={activeTab === tab.id ? 2.5 : 2} />
              <span className="text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-tighter">{tab.label}</span>

          );
