------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/ScrubDial.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import { Key } from "lucide-react";
import { motion } from "motion/react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";

interface ScrubDialProps {
  label: string;
  value: number;
  defaultValue?: number;
  unit?: string;
  step?: number;
  sensitivity?: number;
  hasKey?: boolean;
  onKeyToggle?: () => void;
  onChange: (val: number) => void;
  onCommit: (val: number) => void;
}

export const ScrubDial: React.FC<ScrubDialProps> = ({
  label,
  value,
  defaultValue,
  unit = "",
  step = 1,
  sensitivity = 1,
  hasKey = false,
  onKeyToggle,
  onChange,
  onCommit
}) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [internalValue, setInternalValue] = useState(value);
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState(value.toFixed(2));
  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState(false);
  const [dragStartValue, setDragStartValue] = useState(0);
  const dialRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const lastPosRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  const currentValRef = useRef(value);

  // Sync internal value when not dragging or editing
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isDragging) {
      setInternalValue(value);
      currentValRef.current = value;
    }
  }, [value, isDragging]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isEditing && !isDragging) setInputValue(value.toFixed(2));
  }, [value, isEditing, isDragging, internalValue]);

  const handlePointerDown = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (isEditing) return;
    (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    setIsDragging(true);
    setInternalValue(value);
    currentValRef.current = value;
    setDragStartValue(value);
    lastPosRef.current = e.clientX;
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (!isDragging || lastPosRef.current === null) return;
    
    const movementX = e.clientX - lastPosRef.current;
    lastPosRef.current = e.clientX;

    // 25.4 Dynamic Sensitivity Calculation
    const multiplier = e.shiftKey ? 25 : e.altKey ? 0.1 : 3;
    const delta = movementX * step * sensitivity * multiplier;
    
    currentValRef.current += delta;
    const nextVal = currentValRef.current;
    
    setInternalValue(nextVal);
    setInputValue(nextVal.toFixed(2));
    onChange(nextVal);
  };

  const handlePointerUp = () => {
    if (isDragging) {
      setIsDragging(false);
      lastPosRef.current = null;
      onCommit(currentValRef.current);
    }
  };

  const handleInputChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setInputValue(e.target.value);
  };

  const handleInputBlur = () => {
    setIsEditing(false);
    const parsed = parseFloat(inputValue);
    if (!isNaN(parsed)) {
      onChange(parsed);
      onCommit(parsed);
    }
  };

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === "Enter") {
      (e.target as HTMLInputElement).blur();
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-2 flex flex-col gap-1.5 group select-none">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-1">
        <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-black text-tt-text-muted tracking-widest">{label}</span>
        {onKeyToggle && (
          <button 
            onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onKeyToggle(); }}
            className={cn(
              "p-1 rounded hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors",
              hasKey ? "text-tt-warning drop-shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(255,214,0,0.4)]" : "text-tt-text-muted opacity-40 hover:opacity-100"
            )}
          >
            <Key size={12} fill={hasKey ? "currentColor" : "none"} />
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      <div 
        ref={dialRef}
        className={cn(
          "h-14 bg-tt-bg rounded-md border border-tt-border flex flex-col items-center justify-center cursor-ew-resize relative transition-all touch-none active:border-tt-accent active:shadow-[inset_0_0_15px_rgba(0,120,212,0.1)]",
          isDragging && "border-tt-accent"
        )}
        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
        onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
        onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
      >
        {isEditing ? (
          <input
            id={`scrub-dial-${label}`}
            name={`scrub-dial-${label}`}
            aria-label={`Edit ${label}`}
            autoFocus
            type="text"
            value={inputValue}
            onChange={handleInputChange}
            onBlur={handleInputBlur}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            className="w-full h-full bg-transparent text-center font-mono font-bold text-lg outline-none text-tt-accent"
          />
        ) : (
          <div 
            className="flex flex-col items-center group/value"
            onDoubleClick={(e) => {
              if (e.shiftKey && defaultValue !== undefined) {
                onCommit(defaultValue);
              } else {
                setIsEditing(true);
              }
            }}
          >
            <div className="flex items-baseline gap-0.5 relative">
              <span className="text-xl font-mono font-black tracking-tighter group-hover/value:text-tt-accent transition-colors">
                {Math.round(value * 100) / 100}
              </span>
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted">{unit}</span>
              <span className="absolute -top-3 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 text-[6px] font-black uppercase tracking-tighter text-tt-accent opacity-0 group-hover/value:opacity-100 transition-opacity whitespace-nowrap">
                Shift + 2x Reset
              </span>
            </div>
            
            {/* Visual Feedback: Delta display during drag */}
            {isDragging && (
              <motion.div 
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 5 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                className="absolute -bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 bg-tt-accent text-white text-[8px] px-1.5 rounded-full font-bold"
              >
                {((value - dragStartValue) > 0 ? "+" : "") + (value - dragStartValue).toFixed(1)}
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 25.7 Virtual Dials Pattern */}
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none flex items-center justify-between px-2 opacity-10">
           <div className="w-0.5 h-6 bg-white rounded-full" />
           <div className="flex gap-1">
             {[...Array(5)].map((_, i) => <div key={i} className="w-0.5 h-2 bg-white rounded-full" />)}
           </div>
           <div className="w-0.5 h-6 bg-white rounded-full" />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/SetterModal.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { motion } from "motion/react";
import { X, Mic, Settings, Search, User, Terminal, Send, SquareSquare } from "lucide-react";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface SetterModalProps {
  onClose: () => void;
  contextData: any; // e.g. state layers, selected layer index, etc.
}

export const SetterModal: React.FC<SetterModalProps> = ({ onClose, contextData }) => {
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);
  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState("");
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [log, setLog] = useState<{ type: 'user' | 'system' | 'error' | 'ai', text: string }[]>([
    { type: 'system', text: 'Setter initialized.' }
  ]);
  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);
  const [showSettings, setShowSettings] = useState(false);
  const [engine, setEngine] = useState<'api' | 'workaround'>('api');
  const [apiProvider, setApiProvider] = useState('gemini');
  const [apiKey, setApiKey] = useState('');
  const [webTarget, setWebTarget] = useState('chatgpt');

  // Let's modify the opening log based on the engine
  useEffect(() => {
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { 
       type: 'system', 
       text: `Switched to ${engine === 'api' ? 'API Mode (using built-in Gemini Sandbox API)' : 'Workaround Mode (Proxy Browser Architecture)'}.` 
    }]);
  }, [engine]);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Setup Speech Recognition
    if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
      const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;
      if (SpeechRecognition) {
        recognitionRef.current = new SpeechRecognition();
        recognitionRef.current.continuous = false;
        recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;

        recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {
          let interimTranscript = '';
          let finalTranscript = '';
          for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; ++i) {
            if (event.results[i].isFinal) {
              finalTranscript += event.results[i][0].transcript;
            } else {
              interimTranscript += event.results[i][0].transcript;
            }
          }
          if (finalTranscript) {
            setInputText(prev => prev + (prev ? " " : "") + finalTranscript);
            setIsListening(false);
            // Optionally auto-submit if confident
          } else if (interimTranscript) {
            // We could show interim but for simplicity relying on final
          }
        };

        recognitionRef.current.onend = () => {
          setIsListening(false);
        };
      }
    }
    return () => {
      if (recognitionRef.current) {
        recognitionRef.current.stop();
      }
    };
  }, []);

  const toggleListening = () => {
    if (!recognitionRef.current) {
      alert("Speech recognition not supported in this browser.");
      return;
    }
    if (isListening) {
      recognitionRef.current.stop();
      setIsListening(false);
    } else {
      try {
        recognitionRef.current.start();
        setIsListening(true);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(e);
      }
    }
  };

  const parseContext = () => {
    if (!contextData.activeComp) return "No active composition.";
    const layers = contextData.layers?.map((l: any) => 
      `Layer ${l.index}: "${l.name}" (Type: ${l.layerType}, Selected: ${l.selected})`
    ).join("\n") || "No layers.";
    return `Comp: ${contextData.activeComp.name}\n${layers}`;
  };

  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
  }, [log, isLoading]);

  const handleSend = async () => {
    const text = inputText.trim();
    if (!text) return;
    
    setInputText("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { type: 'user', text }]);
    setIsLoading(true);

    try {
      if (engine === 'workaround') {
        const promptToCopy = `I need an After Effects ExtendScript for this:\n${text}\n\nContext:\n${parseContext()}\n\nPlease provide ONLY the raw ExtendScript code, no markdown format.`;
        
        try {
          await navigator.clipboard.writeText(promptToCopy);
          setLog(prev => [...prev, { 
            type: 'ai', 
            text: `[WM Mode] Prompt copied to clipboard!\n\n1. Paste this into ${webTarget}\n2. Copy the resulting ExtendScript\n3. Start your next message here with "code:" followed by the script to execute it.` 
          }]);
        } catch (err) {
          // Fallback if clipboard API is blocked (e.g. in iframe)
          setLog(prev => [...prev, { 
            type: 'ai', 
            text: `[WM Mode] Could not auto-copy (might be in iframe). Please copy the prompt below:\n\n---\n${promptToCopy}\n---\n\n1. Paste this into ${webTarget}\n2. Copy the resulting ExtendScript\n3. Start your next message here with "code:" followed by the script to execute it.` 
          }]);
        }
        setIsLoading(false);
        return;
      }

      if (text.toLowerCase().startsWith('code:')) {
         const code = text.substring(5).trim();
         socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "eval", script: code });
         setLog(prev => [...prev, { type: 'ai', text: 'Manual code executed!' }]);
         setIsLoading(false);
         return;
      }

      const res = await fetch("/api/setter", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          prompt: text,
          context: parseContext(),
          apiProvider,
          apiKey: apiKey || null
        })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      
      if (data.success && data.script) {
        socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "eval", script: data.script });
        setLog(prev => [...prev, { type: 'ai', text: 'Command generated and sent to AE.' }]);
        
        // Let's add the code snippet for debugging / UX
        setLog(prev => [...prev, { type: 'system', text: `Script: \n${data.script.substring(0, 100)}...` }]);
      } else {
        throw new Error(data.error || "Failed to generate script");
      }
    } catch (e: any) {
      setLog(prev => [...prev, { type: 'error', text: e.message }]);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-[100] flex flex-col md:p-6 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm">
      <motion.div 
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 50, scale: 0.95 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
        exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 50, scale: 0.95 }}
        className="w-full h-full md:max-w-4xl mx-auto flex flex-col bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-none md:rounded-2xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden"
      >
        <div className="h-14 border-b border-tt-border px-4 flex items-center justify-between bg-tt-surface-light shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-tt-accent animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-sm font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-accent">SETTER</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => setShowSettings(!showSettings)} className={`tt-button-icon !p-2 transition-all ${showSettings ? "bg-tt-accent text-white" : "opacity-50 hover:opacity-100"}`} title="Settings">
              <Settings size={16} />
            </button>
            <button onClick={onClose} className="tt-button-icon !p-2 ml-2">
              <X size={18} />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {showSettings && (
          <div className="p-4 bg-tt-surface-light border-b border-tt-border shrink-0 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-top-2">
             <div className="space-y-4 max-w-sm">
                <div>
                   <h3 className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted mb-2">Execution Engine</h3>
                   <div className="flex bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-1">
                      <button 
                        onClick={() => setEngine('api')}
                        className={`flex-1 text-xs py-2 rounded font-bold transition-all ${engine === 'api' ? 'bg-tt-surface shadow text-tt-text' : 'text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text'}`}
                      >
                        API Mode
                      </button>
                      <button 
                        onClick={() => setEngine('workaround')}
                        className={`flex-1 text-xs py-2 rounded font-bold transition-all ${engine === 'workaround' ? 'bg-tt-surface shadow text-tt-text' : 'text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text'}`}
                      >
                        WM
                      </button>
                   </div>
                   <p className="text-[10px] text-tt-text-muted mt-2">
                     {engine === 'api' 
                       ? "Uses direct API keys for seamless script generation." 
                       : "Uses web browser proxy integration (Workaround Mode)."}
                   </p>
                </div>
                
                {engine === 'api' && (
                  <div className="space-y-3">
                    <div>
                      <label className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted mb-1 block">API Provider</label>
                      <select 
                         value={apiProvider} 
                         onChange={e => setApiProvider(e.target.value)}
                         className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-2 text-xs focus:border-tt-accent outline-none text-tt-text"
                      >
                        <option value="gemini" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Google Gemini</option>
                        <option value="openai" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">OpenAI ChatGPT</option>
                        <option value="anthropic" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Anthropic Claude</option>
                        <option value="deepseek" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">DeepSeek v4</option>
                        <option value="qwen" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Qwen AI</option>
                        <option value="doubao" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Doubao AI</option>
                      </select>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <label className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted mb-1 block">API Key</label>
                      <input 
                         type="password" 
                         value={apiKey}
                         onChange={e => setApiKey(e.target.value)}
                         placeholder="Enter API Key or leave empty for default Sandbox" 
                         className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-2 text-xs focus:border-tt-accent outline-none text-tt-text placeholder-tt-text-muted/50" 
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}

                {engine === 'workaround' && (
                  <div className="space-y-3">
                    <div>
                      <label className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted mb-1 block">Web Service Target</label>
                      <select 
                         value={webTarget}
                         onChange={e => setWebTarget(e.target.value)}
                         className="w-full bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-lg p-2 text-xs focus:border-tt-accent outline-none text-tt-text"
                      >
                        <option value="chatgpt" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">ChatGPT Web</option>
                        <option value="claude" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Claude Web</option>
                        <option value="gemini" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">Gemini Web</option>
                        <option value="deepseek" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">DeepSeek Web</option>
                        <option value="huggingface" className="bg-tt-bg text-tt-text">HuggingFace Web</option>
                      </select>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
             </div>
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col p-4 overflow-y-auto gap-3">
          {log.map((msg, i) => (
            <div key={i} className={`flex items-start gap-3 ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'flex-row-reverse' : ''}`}>
              <div className={`shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg ${
                msg.type === 'user' ? 'bg-tt-accent text-white' : 
                msg.type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-500/10 text-red-500 border border-red-500/20' : 
                msg.type === 'ai' ? 'bg-tt-warning text-black' : 'bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border'
              }`}>
                {msg.type === 'user' ? <User size={14} /> : msg.type === 'error' ? <Terminal size={14} /> : msg.type === 'ai' ? <SquareSquare size={14} /> : <Search size={14} />}
              </div>
              <div className={`p-3 rounded-2xl max-w-[80%] text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap ${
                msg.type === 'user' ? 'bg-tt-accent text-white rounded-tr-none' : 
                msg.type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-500/10 text-red-500 border border-red-500/20 font-mono text-xs' : 
                msg.type === 'ai' ? 'bg-tt-surface-light border border-tt-warning/50' :
                'bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border font-mono text-xs opacity-70'
              }`}>
                {msg.text}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
          {isLoading && (
            <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
               <div className="shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-tt-warning text-black flex items-center justify-center animate-bounce shadow-lg w-8 h-8 rounded-full"><SquareSquare size={14} /></div>
               <div className="p-3 bg-tt-surface-light rounded-2xl text-sm italic opacity-50">Thinking...</div>
            </div>
          )}
          <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
        </div>

        <div className="p-4 bg-tt-surface-light border-t border-tt-border shrink-0">
          
          <form className="flex items-center gap-3 relative" onSubmit={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); handleSend(); }}>
            <button 
              type="button"
              onClick={toggleListening}
              className={`w-12 h-12 shrink-0 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg transition-all ${
                isListening ? 'bg-red-500 text-white animate-pulse shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(239,68,68,0.5)]' : 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/20 hover:scale-105'
              }`}
            >
              <Mic size={20} />
            </button>
            <input 
              type="text" 
              value={inputText}
              onChange={(e) => setInputText(e.target.value)}
              disabled={isLoading || isListening}
              placeholder={isListening ? "Listening..." : "Tell After Effects what to do..."}
              className="flex-1 bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border focus:border-tt-accent h-12 rounded-xl px-4 outline-none transition-colors"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit"
              disabled={!inputText.trim() || isLoading}
              className="w-12 h-12 shrink-0 rounded-xl bg-tt-accent hover:bg-tt-accent-hover text-white flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50 transition-all active:scale-95"
            >
              <Send size={18} />
            </button>
          </form>
          <div className="text-center mt-2 text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted">
             {isListening ? 'Speak your command' : 'Type or use voice input'}
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/SpeedPanel.tsx

import React from "react";
import { Timer, Zap, RotateCcw } from "lucide-react";
import { ScrubDial } from "./ScrubDial";
import { Layer } from "@/src/lib/types";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface SpeedPanelProps {
  layer: Layer | null;
}

export const SpeedPanel: React.FC<SpeedPanelProps> = ({ layer }) => {
  if (!layer) return (
    <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
      <Timer size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-10" />
      <p className="text-xs uppercase font-black tracking-widest">Select a layer to adjust speed</p>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="panel-container">
      <div className="h-10 border-b border-tt-border bg-tt-surface-light flex items-center px-4 gap-2">
        <Timer size={14} className="text-tt-accent" />
        <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Time & Speed</span>
      </div>
      
      <div className="scrollable-content p-6 space-y-8">
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-6">
          <ScrubDial 
            label="Time Stretch"
            value={layer.timeStretch || 100}
            unit="%"
            onChange={() => {}}
            onCommit={(val) => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "setTimeStretch", idx: layer.index, value: val })}
          />
          
          <div className="flex gap-3">
             <button className="flex-1 h-12 bg-tt-bg border border-tt-border rounded-xl text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-white/5 flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                <RotateCcw size={16} /> Reset
             </button>
             <button className="flex-1 h-12 bg-tt-accent/10 border border-tt-accent/30 text-tt-accent rounded-xl text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-tt-accent/20 flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                <Zap size={16} /> Enable Remap
             </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="p-4 bg-tt-warning/5 border border-tt-warning/20 rounded-xl space-y-2">
           <h4 className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase text-tt-warning">Pro Tip</h4>
           <p className="text-[10px] text-tt-text-muted italic leading-relaxed">
             Speed adjustments are destructive. Ensure you have backups before applying extreme time stretching.
           </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/TimelineBar.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import {
  Play,
  Pause,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  Clock,
  FastForward,
  Rewind,
  Magnet,
  Grid,
  ZoomIn,
  ZoomOut,
} from "lucide-react";
import { cn, throttle } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

interface TimelineBarProps {
  currentTime: number; // in seconds
  duration: number;
  isPlaying: boolean;
  activeLayer: any;
  onTogglePlay: () => void;
  onSeek: (time: number) => void;
  onStep: (frames: number) => void;
}

export const TimelineBar: React.FC<TimelineBarProps> = ({
  currentTime,
  duration,
  isPlaying,
  activeLayer,
  onTogglePlay,
  onSeek,
  onStep,
}) => {
  const [localTime, setLocalTime] = useState(currentTime || 0);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(1);

  const [isLooping, setIsLooping] = useState(false);
  const playButtonPressTimer = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);

  const [snapEnabled, setSnapEnabled] = useState(true);

  const lastInteractionTime = useRef(0);

  // Sync with prop when not dragging and not immediately after an interaction (prevent bounce)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isDragging && Date.now() - lastInteractionTime.current > 500) {
      setLocalTime(currentTime || 0);
    }
  }, [currentTime, isDragging]);

  const handlePointerDownPlay = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    playButtonPressTimer.current = setTimeout(() => {
      setIsLooping(!isLooping);
      socket.emit("ae_command", {
        command: "executeScript",
        script:
          "if(app.project.activeItem.workAreaDuration===app.project.activeItem.duration){app.project.activeItem.workAreaDuration=app.project.activeItem.duration-0.001}else{app.project.activeItem.workAreaDuration=app.project.activeItem.duration}",
      });
      playButtonPressTimer.current = null;
    }, 1500);
  };

  const handlePointerUpPlay = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (playButtonPressTimer.current) {
      clearTimeout(playButtonPressTimer.current);
      playButtonPressTimer.current = null;
      onTogglePlay();
    }
  };

  const formatTimecode = (seconds: number) => {
    if (!seconds || isNaN(seconds)) seconds = 0;
    const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
    const secs = Math.floor(seconds % 60);
    const frames = Math.floor((seconds % 1) * 30);
    return `${mins.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${secs.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${frames.toString().padStart(2, "0")}`;
  };

  // Build keyframes collection
  const collectedKeys: number[] = [];
  const extractKeys = (props: any[]) => {
    if (!props) return;
    for (const p of props) {
      if (p.keys && Array.isArray(p.keys)) collectedKeys.push(...p.keys);
      if (p.isGroup && p.properties) extractKeys(p.properties);
    }
  };
  if (activeLayer?.rawProperties) {
    extractKeys(activeLayer.rawProperties);
  }
  const uniqueKeys = Array.from(
    new Set(collectedKeys.map((k) => Number(k.toFixed(3)))),
  );

  const safeDuration = duration > 0 ? duration : 10;
  const BASE_WIDTH = 1000;
  const MAX_WIDTH = BASE_WIDTH * zoom;

  const handleScroll = (e: React.UIEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (isPlaying) return; // don't seek from scroll while playing to avoid jerkiness
    const el = e.currentTarget;
    const centerScroll = el.scrollLeft + el.clientWidth / 2;
    // The content width maps to duration
    const time = (centerScroll / MAX_WIDTH) * safeDuration;

    // Optionally snap to keyframes
    let finalTime = Math.max(0, Math.min(safeDuration, time));
    if (snapEnabled && isDragging) {
      let minDiff = 1000;
      let snapT = finalTime;
      for (const k of uniqueKeys) {
        // Mapping time difference to pixel difference to roughly determine snapping sensitivity
        const pixelDiff = (Math.abs(k - finalTime) / safeDuration) * MAX_WIDTH;
        if (pixelDiff < 15 / zoom && pixelDiff < minDiff) {
          minDiff = pixelDiff;
          snapT = k;
        }
      }
      finalTime = snapT;
    }

    setLocalTime(finalTime);
    lastInteractionTime.current = Date.now();

    // Throttle the AE seek during drag for performance
    if (!isDragging) {
      onSeek(finalTime);
    } else {
      throttledSeek(finalTime);
    }
  };

  const throttledSeek = React.useMemo(
    () => throttle((time: number) => onSeek(time), 50),
    [onSeek]
  );

  const handleWheel = (e: React.WheelEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    // Zoom with Ctrl+Scroll or Trackpad Pinch
    if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const zoomFactor = e.deltaY > 0 ? 0.9 : 1.1;
      setZoom(Math.max(0.5, Math.min(zoom * zoomFactor, 10)));
    }
  };

  const handlePointerUp = () => {
    setIsDragging(false);
    lastInteractionTime.current = Date.now();
    onSeek(localTime);
  };

  // Center the scroll based on localTime, but ONLY if we are playing or NOT interacting Native scroll physics break if we set scrollLeft.
  useEffect(() => {
    if (scrollRef.current && (isPlaying || (!isDragging && Date.now() - lastInteractionTime.current > 500))) {
      const targetScroll =
        (localTime / safeDuration) * MAX_WIDTH -
        scrollRef.current.clientWidth / 2;

      // We only update if it drifts significantly to prevent jitter
      if (Math.abs(scrollRef.current.scrollLeft - targetScroll) > 2) {
        scrollRef.current.scrollLeft = targetScroll;
      }
    }
  }, [localTime, isPlaying, isDragging, safeDuration, MAX_WIDTH]);

  // Center playhead on window resize
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleResize = () => {
      if (scrollRef.current) {
        const targetScroll =
          (localTime / safeDuration) * MAX_WIDTH -
          scrollRef.current.clientWidth / 2;
        scrollRef.current.scrollLeft = targetScroll;
      }
    };
    window.addEventListener("resize", handleResize);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", handleResize);
  }, [localTime, safeDuration, MAX_WIDTH]);

  return (
    <div className="h-28 bg-tt-bg border-t border-tt-border flex flex-col shrink-0 overflow-hidden relative">
      {/* Zoom / Info Top Bar */}
      <div className="h-7 bg-tt-surface-light border-b border-tt-border flex items-center px-3 justify-between">
        <div className="text-[10px] text-tt-text-muted font-medium uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5 opacity-60">
          <span>Timeline</span>
          {activeLayer && (
            <>
              <span className="w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-tt-border" />
              <span className="truncate max-w-[120px]">{activeLayer.name}</span>
            </>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <ZoomOut size={12} className="text-tt-text-muted" />
          <input
            type="range"
            min="0.5"
            max="10"
            step="0.1"
            value={zoom}
            onChange={(e) => setZoom(parseFloat(e.target.value))}
            className="w-20 accent-tt-accent h-1 bg-tt-border rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer"
          />
          <ZoomIn size={12} className="text-tt-text-muted" />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Ruler */}
      <div
        ref={scrollRef}
        className="flex-1 overflow-x-auto no-scrollbar relative cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing border-b border-white/5 select-none touch-pan-x"
        onScroll={handleScroll}
        onWheel={handleWheel}
        onPointerDown={() => setIsDragging(true)}
        onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
        onPointerLeave={() => {
          if (isDragging) handlePointerUp();
        }}
      >
        {/* Render a spacer at start and end to allow playhead to reach 0 and max */}
        <div
          style={{ width: `calc(${MAX_WIDTH}px + 100vw)` }}
          className="h-full relative pointer-events-none"
        >
          {/* Ticks Container */}
          <div className="absolute inset-y-0 left-[50vw]">
            {/* Range highlight (composition bounds) */}
            <div
              style={{ width: `${MAX_WIDTH}px` }}
              className="absolute inset-y-0 bg-white/5 border-l border-r border-tt-border/50"
            />
            {/* 1s ticks */}
            <div
              style={{ width: `${MAX_WIDTH}px` }}
              className="absolute inset-y-0 opacity-20 bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,1)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:calc(100%/10)_100%]"
            />
            {/* sub ticks */}
            <div
              style={{ width: `${MAX_WIDTH}px` }}
              className="absolute inset-y-0 opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,1)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:calc(100%/50)_100%]"
            />

            {/* Keyframes */}
            {uniqueKeys.map((k) => (
              <div
                key={k}
                className="absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-2 h-2 rotate-45 border border-tt-accent bg-tt-accent shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(33,150,243,0.8)]"
                style={{
                  left: `${(k / safeDuration) * MAX_WIDTH}px`,
                  marginLeft: "-4px",
                }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Playhead Marker */}
      <div className="absolute top-7 bottom-8 left-1/2 w-[1px] bg-tt-accent shadow-[0_0_12px_rgba(33,150,243,1)] z-10 pointer-events-none" />
      <div className="absolute top-7 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-3 h-3 bg-tt-accent rotate-45 z-10 -mt-1.5 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(33,150,243,0.8)] pointer-events-none" />

      {/* Bottom Controls */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 h-10 bg-tt-bg z-20 relative">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <button
            onClick={() => setSnapEnabled(!snapEnabled)}
            className={cn(
              "p-1.5 rounded transition-colors",
              snapEnabled
                ? "bg-tt-accent/20 text-tt-accent"
                : "text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5",
            )}
            title="Toggle Keyframe Snapping"
          >
            <Magnet size={14} />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => {
              socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "executeScript", script: "app.executeCommand(2366);" });
            }}
            className="p-1.5 text-tt-text-muted hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 rounded transition-colors"
            title="Toggle Proportional Grid (AE)"
          >
            <Grid size={14} />
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="flex flex-1 items-center justify-center gap-3">
          <button
            onClick={() => onSeek(Math.max(0, localTime - 5))}
            className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5"
            title="Rewind 5s"
          >
            <Rewind size={14} />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onStep(-1)}
            className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5"
            title="Previous Frame"
          >
            <ChevronLeft size={16} />
          </button>

          <button
            onPointerDown={handlePointerDownPlay}
            onPointerUp={handlePointerUpPlay}
            onPointerLeave={handlePointerUpPlay}
            className={cn(
              "w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center transition-all active:scale-90",
              isLooping
                ? "bg-tt-warning hover:bg-tt-warning/80"
                : "bg-tt-accent hover:bg-tt-accent-hover",
            )}
            title={
              isLooping
                ? "Looping (Hold to toggle)"
                : "Play (Hold 1.5s for Loop)"
            }
          >
            {isPlaying ? (
              <Pause size={14} fill="white" />
            ) : (
              <Play size={14} fill="white" className="ml-0.5" />
            )}
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={() => onStep(1)}
            className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5"
            title="Next Frame"
          >
            <ChevronRight size={16} />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onSeek(Math.min(safeDuration, localTime + 5))}
            className="tt-button-icon !p-1.5"
            title="Fast Forward 5s"
          >
            <FastForward size={14} />
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 font-mono text-xs text-tt-text-muted bg-tt-surface-light px-2 py-1 rounded-md border border-tt-border">
          <Clock size={12} className="text-tt-accent mr-1" />
          <span className="text-white whitespace-nowrap">
            {formatTimecode(localTime)}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/Trackpad.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { MousePointer2, Move, RotateCw, Maximize, Target } from "lucide-react";
import { cn } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { motion } from "motion/react";

interface TrackpadProps {
  mode: "position" | "anchor" | "scale" | "rotation";
  onDelta: (dx: number, dy: number) => void;
  onCommit: () => void;
}

export const Trackpad: React.FC<TrackpadProps> = ({ mode, onDelta, onCommit }) => {
  const [isActive, setIsActive] = useState(false);
  const [crosshair, setCrosshair] = useState({ x: 50, y: 50 });
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const lastPosRef = useRef<{x: number, y: number} | null>(null);

  const handlePointerDown = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    setIsActive(true);
    lastPosRef.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    updateCrosshair(e);
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (!isActive || !lastPosRef.current) return;
    
    // Calculate movement manually to support touch devices reliably
    const movementX = e.clientX - lastPosRef.current.x;
    const movementY = e.clientY - lastPosRef.current.y;
    lastPosRef.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };

    // 28.4 Scaled Position Mapping
    const multiplier = e.shiftKey ? 5 : e.altKey ? 0.2 : 1;
    onDelta(movementX * multiplier, movementY * multiplier);
    updateCrosshair(e);
  };

  const handlePointerUp = () => {
    setIsActive(false);
    lastPosRef.current = null;
    setCrosshair({ x: 50, y: 50 });
    onCommit();
  };

  const updateCrosshair = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (!containerRef.current) return;
    const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = ((e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width) * 100;
    const y = ((e.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height) * 100;
    setCrosshair({ 
      x: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, x)), 
      y: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, y)) 
    });
  };

  const getIcon = () => {
    switch (mode) {
      case "position": return <Move className="opacity-20" size={48} />;
      case "anchor": return <Target className="opacity-20" size={48} />;
      case "rotation": return <RotateCw className="opacity-20" size={48} />;
      case "scale": return <Maximize className="opacity-20" size={48} />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div 
      ref={containerRef}
      className={cn(
        "relative h-48 sm:h-64 bg-tt-surface border-2 border-tt-border rounded-xl overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair touch-none transition-colors",
        isActive && "border-blue-500 bg-blue-500/5"
      )}
      onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
      onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
      onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
    >
      {/* 28.3 Crosshair Indicator - Removed per user feedback */}
      
      {/* Decorative Grid */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-[0.03] pointer-events-none grid grid-cols-8 grid-rows-8">
        {Array.from({length: 64}).map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="border border-white" />
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center pointer-events-none">
        {getIcon()}
        <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-black tracking-[0.2em] text-tt-text-muted mt-2">
          Trackpad: {mode}
        </span>
      </div>

      <div className="absolute bottom-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[8px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted opacity-50">
         <div className="px-1.5 py-0.5 border border-tt-border rounded">SHIFT ×10</div>
         <div className="px-1.5 py-0.5 border border-tt-border rounded">ALT ×0.1</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/TransformPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useRef } from "react";
import {
  RefreshCw,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronRight,
  Anchor,
  Move,
  RotateCw,
  Maximize,
  Clock,
  Zap,
  Copy,
  ClipboardPaste,
  Box,
} from "lucide-react";
import { cn, throttle } from "@/src/lib/utils";
import { ScrubDial } from "./ScrubDial";
import { Trackpad } from "./Trackpad";
import socket from "@/src/lib/socket";

import { GenericPropertiesPanel } from "./GenericPropertiesPanel";

const throttledEmit = throttle(
  (event: string, data: any) => socket.emit(event, data),
  32,
);

interface GroupProps {
  label: string;
  icon: React.ReactNode;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  defaultExpanded?: boolean;
}

const ControlGroup: React.FC<GroupProps> = ({
  label,
  icon,
  children,
  defaultExpanded = true,
}) => {
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(defaultExpanded);
  return (
    <div className="bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-xl overflow-hidden mb-3">
      <button
        onClick={() => setIsExpanded(!isExpanded)}
        className="w-full h-10 px-3 flex items-center justify-between hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors group"
      >
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-tt-text-muted group-hover:text-tt-text transition-colors">
            {icon}
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-black tracking-widest text-tt-text-muted">
            {label}
          </span>
        </div>
        {isExpanded ? <ChevronDown size={14} /> : <ChevronRight size={14} />}
      </button>
      {isExpanded && (
        <div className="p-3 border-t border-tt-border flex flex-col gap-4 bg-tt-surface/50">
          {children}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export const TransformPanel: React.FC<{ selectedLayer: any }> = ({
  selectedLayer,
}) => {
  const [trackpadMode, setTrackpadMode] = useState<
    "position" | "anchor" | "scale" | "rotation"
  >("position");
  const [activeAxes, setActiveAxes] = useState<{
    x: boolean;
    y: boolean;
    z: boolean;
  }>({ x: true, y: true, z: false });

  const [optimistic, setOptimistic] = useState<any>(null);
  const isInteracting = useRef(false);

  // Sync optimistic when AE updates, unless we are actively dragging
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!isInteracting.current && selectedLayer) {
      setOptimistic({
        pos_x: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.value?.[0] ?? 0,
        pos_y: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.value?.[1] ?? 0,
        pos_z: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.value?.[2] ?? 0,
        anchor_x: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.anchor_point?.value?.[0] ?? 0,
        anchor_y: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.anchor_point?.value?.[1] ?? 0,
        anchor_z: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.anchor_point?.value?.[2] ?? 0,
        scale_x: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.value?.[0] ?? 100,
        scale_y: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.value?.[1] ?? 100,
        scale_z: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.value?.[2] ?? 100,
        rot_x: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.x_rotation?.value ?? 0,
        rot_y: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.y_rotation?.value ?? 0,
        rot: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.rotation?.value ?? 0,
        rot_z:
          selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.z_rotation?.value ??
          selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.rotation?.value ?? 0,
        opacity: selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.opacity?.value ?? 100,
      });
    }
  }, [selectedLayer]);

  if (!selectedLayer || !optimistic) {
    return (
      <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-8 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
        <RefreshCw
          size={48}
          strokeWidth={1}
          className="mb-4 opacity-20 animate-spin"
        />
        <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest font-bold">
          Select a layer to manipulate
        </p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const handlePropertyChange = (prop: string, val: any) => {
    isInteracting.current = true;

    // Optimistic update
    if (prop === "position_x")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, pos_x: val }));
    if (prop === "position_y")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, pos_y: val }));
    if (prop === "position_z")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, pos_z: val }));
    if (prop === "anchor_x")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, anchor_x: val }));
    if (prop === "anchor_y")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, anchor_y: val }));
    if (prop === "anchor_z")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, anchor_z: val }));
    if (prop === "scale") setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, scale_x: val }));
    if (prop === "scale_y") setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, scale_y: val }));
    if (prop === "scale_z") setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, scale_z: val }));
    if (prop === "rotation_x")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, rot_x: val }));
    if (prop === "rotation_y")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, rot_y: val }));
    if (prop === "rotation")
      setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, rot: val, rot_z: val }));
    if (prop === "opacity") setOptimistic((p: any) => ({ ...p, opacity: val }));

    throttledEmit("ae_command", {
      command: "setProperty",
      args: { layerIndex: selectedLayer.index, prop, value: val },
    });
  };

  const handleCommit = (prop: string, val: any) => {
    isInteracting.current = false;
    socket.emit("ae_command", {
      command: "commitProperty",
      args: { layerIndex: selectedLayer.index, prop, value: val },
    });
  };

  return (
    <div className="panel-container">
      <div className="scrollable-content p-4 @container">
        {/* 28. Trackpad Surface */}
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <h3 className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-tt-text-muted">
              Direct Surface
            </h3>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
              <div className="flex bg-tt-surface rounded-md p-0.5 border border-tt-border">
                {(["x", "y", "z"] as const).map((axis) => (
                  <button
                    key={axis}
                    onClick={() =>
                      setActiveAxes((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        [axis]: !prev[axis as keyof typeof prev],
                      }))
                    }
                    className={cn(
                      "px-2 py-1 text-[8px] font-bold uppercase rounded transition-all",
                      activeAxes[axis]
                        ? "bg-tt-accent text-white"
                        : "text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
                      axis === "z" &&
                        !selectedLayer.threeDLayer &&
                        "opacity-30 cursor-not-allowed",
                    )}
                    disabled={axis === "z" && !selectedLayer.threeDLayer}
                  >
                    {axis}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
              <div className="flex bg-tt-surface rounded-md p-0.5 border border-tt-border">
                {(["position", "anchor", "scale", "rotation"] as const).map(
                  (m) => (
                    <button
                      key={m}
                      onClick={() => setTrackpadMode(m)}
                      className={cn(
                        "px-2 py-1 text-[8px] font-bold uppercase rounded transition-all",
                        trackpadMode === m
                          ? "bg-tt-accent text-white"
                          : "text-tt-text-muted hover:text-tt-text",
                      )}
                    >
                      {m}
                    </button>
                  ),
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <Trackpad
            mode={trackpadMode}
            onDelta={(rawDx, rawDy) => {
              isInteracting.current = true;
              let dx = rawDx;
              let dy = rawDy;
              // If only one axis is active, map all movement to that axis
              const activeCount =
                (activeAxes.x ? 1 : 0) +
                (activeAxes.y ? 1 : 0) +
                (activeAxes.z ? 1 : 0);
              if (activeCount === 1) {
                const dominantDelta =
                  Math.abs(rawDx) > Math.abs(rawDy) ? rawDx : rawDy;
                if (activeAxes.x) {
                  dx = dominantDelta;
                  dy = 0;
                }
                if (activeAxes.y) {
                  dy = dominantDelta;
                  dx = 0;
                }
                if (activeAxes.z) {
                  dy = dominantDelta;
                  dx = 0;
                }
              }

              // Optimistic local update
              setOptimistic((p: any) => {
                const next = { ...p };
                if (trackpadMode === "position") {
                  if (activeAxes.x) next.pos_x = (next.pos_x || 0) + dx;
                  if (activeAxes.y) next.pos_y = (next.pos_y || 0) + dy;
                  if (activeAxes.z) next.pos_z = (next.pos_z || 0) + dy;
                } else if (trackpadMode === "anchor") {
                  if (activeAxes.x) next.anchor_x = (next.anchor_x || 0) + dx;
                  if (activeAxes.y) next.anchor_y = (next.anchor_y || 0) + dy;
                  if (activeAxes.z) next.anchor_z = (next.anchor_z || 0) + dy;
                } else if (trackpadMode === "scale") {
                  if (activeAxes.x) next.scale_x = (next.scale_x || 0) + dx;
                  if (activeAxes.y) next.scale_y = (next.scale_y || 0) + dy;
                  if (activeAxes.z) next.scale_z = (next.scale_z || 0) + dy;
                } else if (trackpadMode === "rotation") {
                  // Following socket.ts logic for rotation: dx -> rot_y, dy -> rot_x
                  if (selectedLayer.threeDLayer) {
                    if (activeAxes.x) next.rot_x = (next.rot_x || 0) + dx;
                    if (activeAxes.y) next.rot_y = (next.rot_y || 0) + dy;
                    if (activeAxes.z) next.rot_z = (next.rot_z || 0) + dy;
                  } else {
                    next.rot = (next.rot || 0) + dx;
                    next.rot_z = next.rot;
                  }
                }
                return next;
              });

              throttledEmit("ae_command", {
                command: "deltaProperty",
                args: {
                  layerIndex: selectedLayer.index,
                  mode: trackpadMode,
                  axes: activeAxes,
                  dx,
                  dy,
                },
              });
            }}
            onCommit={() => {
              isInteracting.current = false;
              handleCommit("all", null);
            }}
          />
        </div>

        <div className="flex gap-2 mb-6">
          <button
            onClick={() => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "copyLayer" })}
            className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-xl text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-white/5 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-all active:scale-95"
          >
            <Copy size={14} /> Copy
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "pasteLayer" })}
            className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-surface border border-tt-border rounded-xl text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-white/5 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-all active:scale-95"
          >
            <ClipboardPaste size={14} /> Paste
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() =>
              socket.emit("ae_command", {
                command: "easeProperties",
                idx: selectedLayer.index,
              })
            }
            className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-accent/10 border border-tt-accent/30 text-tt-accent rounded-xl text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-tt-accent/20 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-all active:scale-95"
          >
            <Zap size={14} /> Ease
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() =>
              socket.emit("ae_command", {
                command: "popLayer",
                idx: selectedLayer.index,
              })
            }
            className="flex-1 h-10 bg-tt-warning/10 border border-tt-warning/30 text-tt-warning rounded-xl text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest hover:bg-tt-warning/20 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 transition-all active:scale-95"
          >
            <Maximize size={14} /> Pop
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* 26. Tier 1 Controls */}
        <ControlGroup label="Primary Transform" icon={<Move size={14} />}>
          <div className="flex justify-end mb-2">
            <button
              onClick={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "setLayerProperty",
                  property: "threeDLayer",
                  value: !selectedLayer.threeDLayer,
                  layerIndex: selectedLayer.index,
                })
              }
              className={cn(
                "px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest border transition-all flex items-center gap-2",
                selectedLayer.threeDLayer
                  ? "bg-tt-accent/20 border-tt-accent text-tt-accent shadow-[0_0_10px_rgba(0,120,212,0.2)]"
                  : "bg-tt-bg border-tt-border text-tt-text-muted hover:border-tt-text",
              )}
            >
              <Box size={12} /> 3D Layer
            </button>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <ScrubDial
              label="Position X"
              value={optimistic.pos_x}
              defaultValue={960}
              unit="px"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("position_x", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("position_x", v)}
              hasKey={
                selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.numKeys > 0
              }
              onKeyToggle={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "toggleKeyframes",
                  idx: selectedLayer.index,
                  prop: "position",
                })
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Position Y"
              value={optimistic.pos_y}
              defaultValue={540}
              unit="px"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("position_y", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("position_y", v)}
              hasKey={
                selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.numKeys > 0
              }
              onKeyToggle={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "toggleKeyframes",
                  idx: selectedLayer.index,
                  prop: "position",
                })
              }
            />
            {selectedLayer.threeDLayer && (
              <ScrubDial
                label="Position Z"
                value={optimistic.pos_z}
                defaultValue={0}
                unit="px"
                onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("position_z", v)}
                onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("position_z", v)}
                hasKey={
                  selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.position?.numKeys > 0
                }
                onKeyToggle={() =>
                  socket.emit("ae_command", {
                    command: "toggleKeyframes",
                    idx: selectedLayer.index,
                    prop: "position",
                  })
                }
              />
            )}
            <ScrubDial
              label={
                (selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.value?.length ?? 0) > 2
                  ? "Scale X"
                  : "Scale"
              }
              value={optimistic.scale_x ?? 100}
              defaultValue={100}
              unit="%"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("scale", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("scale", v)}
              hasKey={selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.numKeys > 0}
              onKeyToggle={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "toggleKeyframes",
                  idx: selectedLayer.index,
                  prop: "scale",
                })
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Scale Y"
              value={optimistic.scale_y}
              defaultValue={100}
              unit="%"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("scale_y", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("scale_y", v)}
              hasKey={selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.numKeys > 0}
              onKeyToggle={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "toggleKeyframes",
                  idx: selectedLayer.index,
                  prop: "scale",
                })
              }
            />
            {selectedLayer.threeDLayer && (
              <ScrubDial
                label="Scale Z"
                value={optimistic.scale_z}
                defaultValue={100}
                unit="%"
                onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("scale_z", v)}
                onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("scale_z", v)}
                hasKey={selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.scale?.numKeys > 0}
                onKeyToggle={() =>
                  socket.emit("ae_command", {
                    command: "toggleKeyframes",
                    idx: selectedLayer.index,
                    prop: "scale",
                  })
                }
              />
            )}
            <ScrubDial
              label={selectedLayer.threeDLayer ? "X Rotation" : "Rotation"}
              value={
                selectedLayer.threeDLayer ? optimistic.rot_x : optimistic.rot
              }
              defaultValue={0}
              unit="°"
              sensitivity={0.5}
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("rotation", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("rotation", v)}
              hasKey={
                selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.[
                  selectedLayer.threeDLayer ? "x_rotation" : "rotation"
                ]?.numKeys > 0
              }
              onKeyToggle={() =>
                socket.emit("ae_command", {
                  command: "toggleKeyframes",
                  idx: selectedLayer.index,
                  prop: selectedLayer.threeDLayer ? "x_rotation" : "rotation",
                })
              }
            />
            {selectedLayer.threeDLayer && (
              <>
                <ScrubDial
                  label="Y Rotation"
                  value={optimistic.rot_y}
                  defaultValue={0}
                  unit="°"
                  sensitivity={0.5}
                  onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("y_rotation", v)}
                  onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("y_rotation", v)}
                  hasKey={
                    selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.y_rotation?.numKeys > 0
                  }
                  onKeyToggle={() =>
                    socket.emit("ae_command", {
                      command: "toggleKeyframes",
                      idx: selectedLayer.index,
                      prop: "y_rotation",
                    })
                  }
                />
                <ScrubDial
                  label="Z Rotation"
                  value={optimistic.rot_z}
                  defaultValue={0}
                  unit="°"
                  sensitivity={0.5}
                  onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("z_rotation", v)}
                  onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("z_rotation", v)}
                  hasKey={
                    selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.z_rotation?.numKeys > 0
                  }
                  onKeyToggle={() =>
                    socket.emit("ae_command", {
                      command: "toggleKeyframes",
                      idx: selectedLayer.index,
                      prop: "z_rotation",
                    })
                  }
                />
              </>
            )}
          </div>
        </ControlGroup>

        {/* 27. Tier 2 Controls */}
        <ControlGroup
          label="Geometry & Opacity"
          icon={<Anchor size={14} />}
          defaultExpanded={false}
        >
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <ScrubDial
              label="Anchor X"
              value={optimistic.anchor_x}
              unit="px"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("anchor_x", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("anchor_x", v)}
              hasKey={
                selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.["anchor_point"]?.numKeys >
                0
              }
            />
            <ScrubDial
              label="Anchor Y"
              value={optimistic.anchor_y}
              unit="px"
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("anchor_y", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("anchor_y", v)}
              hasKey={
                selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.["anchor_point"]?.numKeys >
                0
              }
            />
            {selectedLayer.threeDLayer && (
              <ScrubDial
                label="Anchor Z"
                value={optimistic.anchor_z}
                unit="px"
                onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("anchor_z", v)}
                onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("anchor_z", v)}
                hasKey={
                  selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.["anchor_point"]
                    ?.numKeys > 0
                }
              />
            )}
            <ScrubDial
              label="Opacity"
              value={optimistic.opacity}
              unit="%"
              step={0.5}
              onChange={(v) => handlePropertyChange("opacity", v)}
              onCommit={(v) => handleCommit("opacity", v)}
              hasKey={selectedLayer.properties?.transform?.opacity?.numKeys > 0}
            />
          </div>
        </ControlGroup>

        <ControlGroup
          label="Time & Velocity"
          icon={<Clock size={14} />}
          defaultExpanded={false}
        >
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-tt-text-muted">
                Motion Blur
              </span>
              <button className="tt-button-icon !p-1 text-tt-accent bg-tt-accent/10">
                <Zap size={14} />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </ControlGroup>

        <GenericPropertiesPanel layer={selectedLayer} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export const VolumePanel: React.FC<VolumePanelProps> = ({ layer }) => {
  if (!layer || !layer.flags.audio) return (
    <div className="panel-container items-center justify-center p-12 text-center text-tt-text-muted">
      <Volume2 size={48} strokeWidth={1} className="mb-4 opacity-10" />

    </div>
  );

      </div>
      
      <div className="scrollable-content p-6 space-y-8">
        <div className="space-y-6">

             onClick={() => socket.emit("ae_command", { command: "executeScript", script: `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c) { var l = c.layer(${layer.index}); if (l) l.audioEnabled = !l.audioEnabled; }` })}
             className={`w-full h-14 ${layer.flags.solo ?             <VolumeX size={20} />
            Toggle Audio Layer
          </button>
        </div>

        <GenericPropertiesPanel layer={layer} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/hooks/useLongPress.ts
------------------------------------------------------------

import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';

export function useLongPress(
  onLongPress: (e: any) => void,
  onClick: (e: any) => void,
  { delay = 300, shouldPreventDefault = true } = {}
) {
  const [longPressTriggered, setLongPressTriggered] = useState(false);
  const timeout = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);
  const target = useRef<any>(null);

  const start = useCallback(
    (e: any) => {
      if (shouldPreventDefault && e.target) {
        e.target.addEventListener('touchend', preventDefault, {
          passive: false
        });
        target.current = e.target;
      }
      timeout.current = setTimeout(() => {
        onLongPress(e);
        setLongPressTriggered(true);
      }, delay);
    },
    [onLongPress, delay, shouldPreventDefault]
  );

  const clear = useCallback(
    (e: any, shouldTriggerClick = true) => {
      timeout.current && clearTimeout(timeout.current);
      shouldTriggerClick && !longPressTriggered && onClick(e);
      setLongPressTriggered(false);
      if (shouldPreventDefault && target.current) {
        target.current.removeEventListener('touchend', preventDefault);
      }
    },
    [onClick, longPressTriggered, shouldPreventDefault]
  );

  return {
    onMouseDown: (e: any) => start(e),
    onTouchStart: (e: any) => start(e),
    onMouseUp: (e: any) => clear(e),
    onMouseLeave: (e: any) => clear(e, false),
    onTouchEnd: (e: any) => clear(e)
  };
}

const preventDefault = (e: any) => {
  if (!e.cancelable) return;
  e.preventDefault();
};

FILE: src/lib/socket.ts
