type Callback = (...args: any[]) => void;

class SocketWrapper {
  private ws: WebSocket | null = null;
  private listeners: Record<string, Callback[]> = {};
  private reconnectTimer: any = null;

  constructor() {
    this.connect();
  }

  private connect() {
    // In dev mode via Vite the host is same, inside docker it's standard port
    const protocol = window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:';
    const host = window.location.host;
    this.ws = new WebSocket(`${protocol}//${host}/`);

    this.ws.onopen = () => {
      console.log("[WebSocket] Connected to Server");
      this.triggerLocal("connect");
    };

    this.ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      try {
        const msg = JSON.parse(event.data);
        
        // Translate the user's bridge protocol to our frontend events
        if (msg.type === "bridge_status") {
          this.triggerLocal("ae_status", { connected: msg.connected });
        } else if (msg.type === "status" && msg.message === "sync" && msg.state) {
          // This is our auto-sync
          this.triggerLocal("ui_state_update", msg.state);
        } else if (msg.type === "result" || msg.type === "error") {
          this.triggerLocal("response", msg);
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error("WS Parse error", e);
      }
    };

    this.ws.onclose = () => {
      console.log("[WebSocket] Disconnected. Reconnecting...");
      this.triggerLocal("disconnect");
      this.triggerLocal("ae_status", { connected: false });
      clearTimeout(this.reconnectTimer);
      this.reconnectTimer = setTimeout(() => this.connect(), 2000);
    };
  }

  on(event: string, callback: Callback) {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) this.listeners[event] = [];
    this.listeners[event].push(callback);
  }

  off(event: string, callback?: Callback) {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) return;
    if (callback) {
      this.listeners[event] = this.listeners[event].filter(cb => cb !== callback);
    } else {
      this.listeners[event] = [];
    }
  }

  triggerLocal(event: string, ...args: any[]) {
    if (this.listeners[event]) {
      this.listeners[event].forEach(cb => cb(...args));
    }
  }

  emit(event: string, data?: any) {
    if (!this.ws || this.ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) return;
    this.processCommandAndSend(event, data, Date.now().toString() + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000));
  }

  request(event: string, data?: any): Promise<any> {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      if (!this.ws || this.ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
        return reject(new Error("WebSocket not open"));
      }
      const reqId = Date.now().toString() + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);
      
      const handler = (msg: any) => {
        if (msg.reqId === reqId) {
          this.off("response", handler);
          if (msg.type === "error") reject(new Error(msg.error));
          else resolve(msg.data);
        }
      };
      this.on("response", handler);
      
      // timeout after 15s
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.off("response", handler);
        reject(new Error("Request timed out"));
      }, 15000);

      this.processCommandAndSend(event, data, reqId);
    });
  }

  private processCommandAndSend(event: string, data: any, reqId: string) {
    if (event === "identify") {
      this.ws!.send(JSON.stringify({ action: "identify", role: data }));
    } else if (event === "ae_command" && data) {
      // We must translate our "command" to the user's "action" format
      let actionObj = { ...data };
      if (actionObj.command) {
        let action = actionObj.command;
        
        // Map frontend commands to bridge.jsx actions
        if (action === "togglePlay") action = "playPause";
        else if (action === "updateComp") {
           actionObj = { ...actionObj, ...actionObj.args };
           action = "setCompSettings";
           delete actionObj.args;
        } else if (action === "addLayer") {
           const t = actionObj.type?.toLowerCase() || "";
           if (t === "solid") action = "createSolid";
           else if (t === "text") action = "createText";
           else if (t === "shape") action = "createShape";
           else if (t === "null") action = "createNull";
           else if (t === "camera") action = "createCamera";
           else if (t === "light") action = "createLight";
        } else if (action === "setEffectProperty") {
           action = "executeScript";
           actionObj.script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${actionObj.idx}); var e=l.property('Effects').property('${actionObj.effect.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}'); if(e){var p=e.property('${actionObj.prop.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}'); if(p)p.setValue(${actionObj.value});}}`;
         } else if (action === "setProperty" || action === "commitProperty") {
           action = "executeScript";
           const prop = actionObj.args.prop;
           const val = actionObj.args.value;
           const layerIdx = actionObj.args.layerIndex;
           
           let script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${layerIdx}); var p; var v;`;
           
           if (prop.startsWith("position")) {
               const axis = prop === "position_x" ? 0 : prop === "position_y" ? 1 : 2;
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Position'); v=p.value; v[${axis}]=${val}; p.setValue(v);`;
           } else if (prop.startsWith("anchor")) {
               const axis = prop === "anchor_x" ? 0 : prop === "anchor_y" ? 1 : 2;
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Anchor Point'); var pos=l.property('Transform').property('Position'); var sc=l.property('Transform').property('Scale'); v=p.value; var pv=pos.value; var sv=sc.value; var delta=${val}-v[${axis}]; v[${axis}]=${val}; pv[${axis}]+=delta*(sv[${axis}]!==undefined?sv[${axis}]/100:1); p.setValue(v); pos.setValue(pv);`;
           } else if (prop === "scale") {
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Scale'); v=p.value; p.setValue([${val},${val},${val}]);`;
           } else if (prop.startsWith("scale_")) {
               const axis = prop === "scale_x" ? 0 : prop === "scale_y" ? 1 : 2;
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Scale'); v=p.value; v[${axis}]=${val}; p.setValue(v);`;
           } else if (prop === "rotation" || prop === "z_rotation") {
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Rotation') || l.property('Transform').property('Z Rotation'); if(p) p.setValue(${val});`;
           } else if (prop === "x_rotation") {
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('X Rotation'); if(p) p.setValue(${val});`;
           } else if (prop === "y_rotation") {
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Y Rotation'); if(p) p.setValue(${val});`;
           } else if (prop === "opacity") {
               script += `p=l.property('Transform').property('Opacity'); if(p) p.setValue(${val});`;
           }
           script += "}";
           actionObj.script = script;
           delete actionObj.args;
        } else if (action === "undo") {
           action = "undo";
        } else if (action === "redo") {
           action = "redo";
        } else if (action === "setBlending") {
           action = "setBlendMode";
           const modes = ["Normal", "Dissolve", "Dancing Dissolve", "Darken", "Multiply", "Color Burn", "Linear Burn", "Darker Color", "Lighten", "Screen", "Color Dodge", "Linear Dodge", "Lighter Color", "Overlay", "Soft Light", "Hard Light", "Linear Light", "Vivid Light", "Pin Light", "Hard Mix", "Difference", "Exclusion", "Subtract", "Divide"];
           // We expect actionObj.mode to be 1-based index from frontend
           actionObj.mode = modes[(actionObj.mode||1)-1] || "Normal";
        } else if (action === "toggleInvert") {
           action = "executeScript";
           actionObj.script = "var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var m=c.layer(" + (actionObj.idx||1) + ").property('ADBE Mask Parade').property(" + (actionObj.maskIndex||1) + "); if(m) m.property('ADBE Mask Inverted').setValue(!m.property('ADBE Mask Inverted').value);}";
        } else if (action === "removeMask") {
           action = "executeScript";
           actionObj.script = "var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var m=c.layer(" + (actionObj.idx||1) + ").property('ADBE Mask Parade').property(" + (actionObj.maskIndex||1) + "); if(m) m.remove();}";
        } else if (action === "deltaProperty") {
           action = "executeScript";
           const mode = actionObj.args.mode;
           const axes = actionObj.args.axes || {x: true, y: true, z: false};
           const dx = actionObj.args.dx;
           const dy = actionObj.args.dy;
           const layerIdx = actionObj.args.layerIndex;
           
           let propName = 'Position';
           if (mode === 'anchor') propName = 'Anchor Point';
           else if (mode === 'scale') propName = 'Scale';
           else if (mode === 'rotation') propName = 'Rotation';
           
           if (mode === 'rotation') {
             // For rotation, we apply dx to Y rotation, dy to X rotation, unless only specific ones are chosen. Or we just keep it simple: 
             // If 3D, rotation has X/Y/Z explicitly. But Trackpad in TouchTools mode usually drove standard rotation.
             // If axes.z is true, drive Z Rotation, else X/Y.
             actionObj.script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${layerIdx});
               if(l.threeDLayer){
                  if(${axes.x}) { var px=l.property('Transform').property('X Rotation'); px.setValue(px.value + ${dx}); }
                  if(${axes.y}) { var py=l.property('Transform').property('Y Rotation'); py.setValue(py.value + ${dy}); }
                  if(${axes.z}) { var pz=l.property('Transform').property('Z Rotation'); pz.setValue(pz.value + ${dx + dy}); }
               } else {
                 var p=l.property('Transform').property('Rotation'); p.setValue(p.value + (${dx} + ${dy}));
               }
             }`;
           } else if (mode === 'anchor') {
             actionObj.script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${layerIdx}); var a=l.property('Transform').property('Anchor Point'); var p=l.property('Transform').property('Position'); var s=l.property('Transform').property('Scale'); var av=a.value; var pv=p.value; var sv=s.value; if(${axes.x}){av[0]+=${dx}; pv[0]+=${dx}*(sv[0]/100);} if(${axes.y}){av[1]+=${dy}; pv[1]+=${dy}*(sv[1]/100);} if(${axes.z} && l.threeDLayer){av[2]+=${dy}; pv[2]+=${dy}*(sv[2]?sv[2]/100:1);} a.setValue(av); p.setValue(pv);}`;
           } else {
             actionObj.script = `var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(${layerIdx}); var p=l.property('Transform').property('${propName}'); var v=p.value; if(${axes.x}) v[0]+=${dx}; if(${axes.y}) v[1]+=${dy}; if(${axes.z} && v.length > 2) v[2]+=${dy}; p.setValue(v);}`;
           }
           delete actionObj.args;
        } else if (action === "easeProperties" || action === "copyLayer" || action === "pasteLayer" || action === "popLayer" || action === "step" || action === "seek" || action === "toggleKeyframes" || action === "eval") {
           action = "executeScript";
           if (actionObj.command === "seek") actionObj.script = "if(app.project && app.project.activeItem) app.project.activeItem.time = " + actionObj.time + ";";
           else if (actionObj.command === "step") actionObj.script = "if(app.project && app.project.activeItem){var c=app.project.activeItem; c.time += " + actionObj.frames + " * (1/c.frameRate);}";
           else if (actionObj.command === "copyLayer") actionObj.script = "app.executeCommand(19);"; // Edit > Copy
           else if (actionObj.command === "pasteLayer") actionObj.script = "app.executeCommand(20);"; // Edit > Paste
           else if (actionObj.command === "eval") actionObj.script = actionObj.script; // Keep user script
           else if (actionObj.command === "toggleKeyframes") {
             const propMap: Record<string, string> = { "position": "Position", "scale": "Scale", "rotation": "Rotation", "x_rotation": "X Rotation", "y_rotation": "Y Rotation", "z_rotation": "Z Rotation", "anchor_point": "Anchor Point", "opacity": "Opacity" };
             const mappedProp = propMap[actionObj.prop] || actionObj.prop;
             actionObj.script = "var c=app.project.activeItem; if(c){var l=c.layer(" + actionObj.idx + "); if(l){var p=l.property('Transform').property('" + mappedProp + "'); if(p){if(p.numKeys>0){while(p.numKeys) p.removeKey(1);} else {p.setValueAtTime(c.time, p.value);}}}}";
           }
           else if (!actionObj.script) actionObj.script = "// not fully implemented yet";
        } else if (action === "refresh") {
           return; // Sync handles this automatically
        }

        actionObj.action = action;
        delete actionObj.command;
      }
      
      this.ws!.send(JSON.stringify({
        action: "sendToAE",
        command: {
          reqId,
          ...actionObj
        }
      }));
    }
  }
}

const socket = new SocketWrapper();
export default socket;

export type LayerType = 
  | "AV" 
  | "Shape" 
  | "Text" 
  | "Camera" 
  | "Light" 
  | "Adjustment" 
  | "Null" 
  | "Solid";

export interface Property {
  name: string;
  matchName: string;
  value: any;
  hasKeyframes: boolean;
  canBeKeyframed: boolean;
  type: "Number" | "Array2D" | "Array3D" | "Color" | "Boolean" | "String" | "Custom";
}

export interface Layer {
  index: number;
  name: string;
  type: LayerType;
  layerType?: string;
  visible: boolean;
  selected: boolean;
  expanded?: boolean;
  flags: {
    solo: boolean;
    lock: boolean;
    shy: boolean;
    motionBlur: boolean;
    effects: boolean;
    audio: boolean;
    guide: boolean;
  };
  blendingMode?: number;
  blendMode?: string;
  threeDLayer?: boolean;
  rawProperties?: any;
  timeStretch?: number;
  inPoint?: number;
  outPoint?: number;
  masks?: {
    name: string;
    mode: number;
    inverted: boolean;
  }[];
  effects?: {
    name: string;
    enabled: boolean;
    properties: {
      name: string;
      value: any;
      hasKeyframes: boolean;
    }[];
  }[];
  properties: {
    transform: {
      anchorPoint: Property;
      position: Property;
      scale: Property;
      rotation: Property;
      opacity: Property;
    };
    audio?: {
      levels: Property;
    };
  };
}

export interface Composition {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  pixelAspect?: number;
  frameRate?: number;
  duration?: number;
  workAreaStart?: number;
  workAreaDuration?: number;
}

export interface AppState {
  connected: boolean;
  activeComp: Composition | null;
  compositions: Composition[];
  layers: Layer[];
  selectedLayerIndex: number | null;
  activeTab: string;
  time: number;
  isXMode: boolean;
}

FILE: src/lib/utils.ts

import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}

export function throttle<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(func: T, limit: number): T {
  let inThrottle: boolean;
  let lastResult: ReturnType<T>;
  return function(this: any, ...args: Parameters<T>): ReturnType<T> {
    if (!inThrottle) {
      inThrottle = true;
      setTimeout(() => (inThrottle = false), limit);
      lastResult = func.apply(this, args);
    }
    return lastResult;
  } as T;
}

import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';
import {defineConfig, loadEnv} from 'vite';

export default defineConfig(({mode}) => {
  const env = loadEnv(mode, '.', '');
  return {
    plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
    define: {
      'process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY': JSON.stringify(env.GEMINI_API_KEY),
    },
    resolve: {
      alias: {
        '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '.'),
      },
    },
    server: {
      hmr: false,
      watch: process.env.DISABLE_HMR === 'true' ? null : {},
    },
  };
});
